Time Management Analysis (v1.0.3 upgrade)

From v1.0.3, the time-management module is upgraded from v1.0.2's "only shows [%clk] counts" to a full time analysis. The new extractMoveTimes() function auto-detects time data inside PGN comment {}, supporting the following formats (by recognition priority):

  1. v1.0.3 direct format: {3.2s +0.5 Slight edge} (time + space + eval). This is the format used by the app itself when exporting PGN from v1.0.3 onward. extractMoveTimes() takes the first number+s pattern in the comment as the move's time. No header required.
  2. Standard PGN clock format (requires [TimeControl] header): [%clk HH:MM:SS] indicates the player's remaining clock time after completing the move. The app uses the [TimeControl "BASE+INC"] header to derive per-move actual time. Supports "7200+60" (base + increment), "1800" (base only, no increment), "40/7200" (7200 seconds for 40 moves, treated as no-increment) formats. Without [TimeControl] header, [%clk] only records the clock remaining value without deriving time.
  3. Legacy dash format: {3.2s——+0.5 Slight edge} (time + dash + eval). Backward-compatible — early v1.0.3 test versions of exported PGN still parse correctly.

Display Content

  • Total time / White time / Black time: tri-color stat cards
  • Average per move / White average / Black average: per-move average time
  • Longest time move: includes move number (e.g. "5." or "5...") and time
  • Shortest time move: includes move number and time
  • Time variance: standard deviation, reflecting time-distribution dispersion
  • Long-thinking moves (>10s): count of moves exceeding 10 seconds
  • Quick moves (<1s): count of moves under 1 second
  • Per-phase time ratio: Opening (first 20 moves) / Middlegame (21-60 moves) / Endgame (61+ moves)
  • Per-move time bar chart: SVG bar chart; White moves use white bars, Black moves use blue bars

Clicking Variation Moves for Variation Stats (v1.0.3 NEW)

In v1.0.2, only main-line moves were clickable for per-position stats. From v1.0.3, variation moves inside () are also clickable. When a variation move is clicked, the stats page constructs a synthetic move sequence per the following rules:

  1. Take main-line moves [0..mainIdxBefore-1], where mainIdxBefore is the index of the main-line move immediately to the left of () (i.e. the move being replaced by the variation's first move).
  2. Append variation moves [0..clickedIdx] (from the variation's first move to the clicked move). Variation moves are re-parsed via applySANMove() (supports castling, promotion, capture, disambiguation, etc.).
  3. Recompute all statistics modules with the synthetic sequence.

For example, in PGN 1. e4 e5 2. Nf3 (2. Bc4 Nf6 3. d3) Nc6, clicking variation's 3. d3:

  • mainIdxBefore = 3 (i.e. main-line move 4 Nf3 at index 3)
  • Synthetic sequence = first 3 main-line moves [e4, e5, Nf3] + first 3 variation moves [Bc4, Nf6, d3] = 6 moves
  • Stats modules show position stats after 3.d3

Position FEN Panel (v1.0.3 NEW)

The Position FEN panel is below the PGN text panel, showing the FEN string of the position immediately after the currently selected move. The FEN is auto-generated by the background stateToFEN() function from the selected move's postState, including 6 fields:

  1. Board placement (rank 8 → rank 1, /-separated, empty squares as digits)
  2. Side to move (w or b)
  3. Castling rights (KQkq or -; Chess960 uses Shredder-FEN format like HAah)
  4. En-passant target square (e.g. e3 or -)
  5. Halfmove clock
  6. Fullmove number

Statistics Page Board Coord Labels (v1.0.4 Rev41 fix) v1.0.4 Rev41

v1.0.4 Rev41 refactors the statistics page board's coord label layout to be fully consistent with the main UI board:

  • Letters a-h moved outside the board top: file labels (a-h) moved from inside the board to above the board, matching the main UI's .flbl style (font size .7rem, color var(--muted), system-ui font, letter-spacing:1px)
  • Numbers 1-8 moved outside the board left: rank labels (1-8) moved from inside the board to the left of the board, matching the main UI's .rlbl style (same font size/color/font, flex column layout)
  • Each square shows coord label inside: each square's top-left shows a coord label (e.g. e4), fully consistent with the main UI's .sq .lbl style — position absolute top:1px left:2px, font size 9px, opacity .95, DejaVu Sans font, LBL_LIGHT/LBL_DARK colors, .6px stroke, text-shadow glow, paint-order:stroke fill

Heatmap Control Statistics v1.0.4

The statistics page adds a "Heatmap Control Statistics" block, walking every real position in the game (including the initial position and after each move), computing per-square attacker counts for both sides, cached by FEN to avoid duplicate computation.

  • Renders an 8×8 average-control heatmap: each square shows (White avg / Black avg) attacker count, with HSL background indicating net control (blue = White-leaning, red = Black-leaning, purple = contested)
  • Adds "White/Black Strongest Square" and "White/Black Weakest Square" stats, ranked by average control across all positions
  • Adds "Center White/Black Average" and "Center Net (W-B)", computed as the mean over d4/e4/d5/e5
  • v1.0.4 Rev34 NEW: each cell of the heatmap control statistics matrix now shows a coord label (e.g. a8, e4) at the top center, making it easy to identify which board square each heatmap cell represents

Web Worker Parallel Computation v1.0.4

v1.0.4 adds the worker-pool.js module, offloading PGN parsing, statistics computation, and control-map computation to a Web Worker thread to avoid blocking UI rendering:

  • Worker is created via a Blob URL (compatible with WebView's script-src 'unsafe-inline' CSP)
  • Ships with a slim copy of chess primitives (attacked, getCtrlMap, makeMvInPlace, fenToState, etc.) — no shared scope with the main thread
  • All public APIs (workerParsePGN, workerComputeHeatmapStats, workerGetCtrlMap) return Promises
  • If Worker is unavailable (very old devices), auto-falls back to inline synchronous execution, guaranteeing feature parity
  • v1.0.4 Rev44 Memory-leak fix: added terminateWorker() function registered on pagehide and beforeunload events. On page exit, terminates the Worker and revokes its Blob URL to prevent memory leaks

Implementation Details: Stats Page Architecture

The statistics page launches a new StatsActivity via openStatsPage(), passing the main app's already-parsed authoritative move records (from/to/piece/captured/promotion/notation). The stats page replays these moves directly via parseFromMoveRecords() (using executeMove() to correctly advance state), completely bypassing the simplified SAN parser. For paste/import PGN scenarios (no move records), it falls back to the simplified parser.

v1.0.4 Rev34 fixes Chess960 compatibility: applySANMove() no longer hardcodes King start column 4 (e1), instead scanning the back rank for the King's actual column. executeMove() no longer always takes the rook from column 7 (h1) or column 0 (a1), instead scanning for the nearest rook in the castling direction.

stats.html — Chess960-compatible castling detection // Old version (standard-chess only) function isCastling(from, to) { return Math.abs(to.col - from.col) === 2; } // v1.0.4 Rev34 fix (target-column detection, Chess960-compatible) function isCastling(from, to) { // Target column 6 = kingside (O-O), target column 2 = queenside (O-O-O) // In Chess960 King start position varies, but final squares are fixed at g1/c1 return to.col === 6 || to.col === 2; } // Chess960-compatible rook move function moveRookForCastling(state, kingFrom, kingTo) { // Scan for the nearest rook in the castling direction const side = kingTo.col === 6 ? 'kingside' : 'queenside'; const dir = side === 'kingside' ? 1 : -1; let rookCol = -1; for (let c = kingFrom.col + dir; c >= 0 && c <= 7; c += dir) { if (state.board[kingFrom.row][c] && state.board[kingFrom.row][c].type === 'rook') { rookCol = c; break; } } if (rookCol === -1) return; // No rook found (fall back to standard position) const rookTo = side === 'kingside' ? 5 : 3; state.board[kingFrom.row][rookTo] = state.board[kingFrom.row][rookCol]; state.board[kingFrom.row][rookCol] = null; }

💾HTML Export Changed to Static Snapshot

The 💾HTML button no longer copies the entire page (with JS code); instead it outputs a pure static HTML file — containing only the current selected state's UI and statistics data (CSS + content), without any <script> tags, functions, or interfaces. The exported file can be opened in any browser, frozen at the export-time selected state.

v1.0.4 Rev43 fixes a critical bug where exported HTML was stuck at "Loading": the original _stripFnBody() used brace-counting that truncated at nested functions. Rev43 changed to a regex approach function name(){...} → function name(){}. Rev44 further simplified via non-greedy match to next line-start \n}.

Chapter 16
Ponder Implementation Mechanism

The Ponder feature is implemented based on the go ponder command of the UCI (Universal Chess Interface) protocol. This chapter details the complete data flow, the four-layer protection mechanism, and time-control compliance.

Complete Data Flow

  1. Engine returns best move: the engine outputs bestmove e2e4 ponder e7e5 via stdout, where e2e4 is the recommended move and e7e5 is the engine's predicted opponent reply.
  2. Java-layer parsing: StockfishNative.processEngineLine() uses the regex ^bestmove\s+(\S+)(?:\s+ponder\s+(\S+))? to parse the ponder move, storing it in the _lastPonderMove field. If no ponder field is present, it is set to null.
  3. JS-layer obtains ponder data: both onBestMove() and onHintMove() obtain the current ponder move via AndroidBridge.getLastPonderMove(). getLastPonderMove() is a one-time read (auto-clears after read), preventing stale data from leaking into subsequent searches. The UCI move is temporarily stored in _pendingPonderMoveUCI, waiting for the first onPonderProgress() callback to convert to SAN format and assign to _ponderMoveSAN.
  4. Start ponder search: after the AI moves, onBestMove() applies the ponder move to the current position (simulating the opponent's move via makeMv()), generates a new FEN, and calls AndroidBridge.startPonder(fen). The Java layer sends position fen <FEN> and go ponder to the engine, entering infinite-search mode.
  5. Ponder progress callback and delayed conversion: while searching, the engine calls back onPonderProgress() in real time via info lines, updating _ponderBarInfo (search depth, node count, eval). On the first callback, if _pendingPonderMoveUCI exists, it is converted to SAN and assigned to _ponderMoveSAN (one-time, cleared after conversion). This delayed mechanism ensures the ponder move and search progress appear at the same time, avoiding incomplete UI display.
  6. Ponder Hit / Stop: when the player moves, executeMove() checks whether it matches the ponder move. On match, calls AndroidBridge.ponderHit() (engine uses existing search results to continue analysis); on mismatch, calls AndroidBridge.stopPonder() (engine stops searching).
  7. Display conditions: the AI Opponent Bar row 3 shows 🔮 ponder info only when both _ponderMoveSAN (SAN-format ponder move) and _ponderBarInfo (search progress) exist. When the AI is thinking, hint-loading, in review mode, or when the game ends, it is auto-hidden.

Four-Layer Protection Mechanism

Regalia uses four layers of protection to ensure Ponder data does not retain stale information:

  1. Generation Counter: the JS-layer core defense — all onPonderProgress() callbacks must pass generation validation before updating display data. Each new ponder session increments _ponderGen++; on callback, if _ponderGen !== _ponderStartGen, the callback is discarded.
  2. One-time read: getLastPonderMove() auto-clears after read, preventing old ponder moves from leaking into subsequent searches.
  3. Immediate DOM update: when clearing ponder variables, immediately calls _updateAIThinkDisplay() to avoid stale DOM values after variable clearing.
  4. Java-layer flag: the _discardingPonderBestmove flag prevents the post-ponder-stop bestmove from being incorrectly routed to the normal search processing flow.

UCI Ponder Interaction Example

UCI Ponder Interaction Example // AI plays Nf3, engine predicts opponent will play e5 → position startpos moves e2e4 e7e5 g1f3 → go ponder // engine enters infinite search ← info depth 15 ... pv e7e5 d2d4 ... // onPonderProgress() updates in real time // Player played e5 (matches ponder prediction) → ponderhit // engine immediately uses existing analysis ← bestmove d2d4 ponder b8c6 // nearly zero-latency next-move response // If player plays a different move (mismatch with prediction) → stop // engine stops searching ← bestmove ... // discard ponder result, re-analyze

Ponder Display in Hint Scenario

In the hint scenario, onHintMove() directly converts the ponder move to SAN and embeds it in hintText, displaying it alongside the recommended move (e.g. "🔦 Hint: Nf3 🔮 Ponder: e5") without waiting for Ponder search progress. Conditional display:

  • AI Hint bar: when the user requests a hint (💡 AI Hint), if the engine's bestmove is followed by ponder info, the hint text shows both the recommended move and the ponder move
  • AI Opponent Bar row 3: shows ponder info when the engine's background Ponder search is active
  • No ponder info: no Ponder-related content is shown, keeping the UI clean

Ponder Data Timeliness

Ponder info always comes from the ponder field of the most recent bestmove response. Each time the engine returns a new bestmove, the old ponder data is immediately cleared, and the display is updated only when the new bestmove contains ponder info, ensuring ponder data does not retain stale info. In the hint scenario, the ponder move is converted to SAN format when the engine returns bestmove (converted based on the position after the recommended move is executed, ensuring move correctness), directly embedded in the hint text without waiting for the Ponder search progress callback.

Anti-Stale-Data Mechanism (Multi-layer Protection)

  1. Each time ponder variables are cleared, immediately call _updateAIThinkDisplay() to update the DOM, avoiding stale DOM values after variable clearing
  2. onPonderProgress() adds a generation guard (_ponderGen / _ponderStartGen); if the current callback's generation differs from the start, ponder has been cleared by another flow and the callback should be discarded
  3. onEngineProgress() actively clears residual ponder data during AI thinking or hint loading
  4. Java layer adds the _discardingPonderBestmove flag, preventing the post-ponder-stop bestmove from being incorrectly routed to the normal search processing flow
  5. The hint area now requires both _ponderMoveSAN and _ponderBarInfo to display 🔮 ponder, avoiding stale ponder data being shown after a new ponder session starts but before the first progress frame arrives

Time Control Ponder Compliance v1.0.4 Rev31

The original startPonder() only sent "go ponder" without time parameters — violating the UCI spec. The UCI spec requires go ponder to include wtime/btime/winc/binc parameters so the engine can switch to normal timed search on receiving ponderhit. Rev31 fix: startPonder() takes 4 new time parameters; JS passes the current gameClocks values. For non-time-control games, all-zeros are passed, and Java detects this and sends "go ponder" (without time parameters). The @deprecated single-argument startPonder(fen) overload is retained for backward compatibility.

Ponder Score Perspective Fix v1.0.4 Rev36

Rev36 fixes a serious bug in onPonderProgress score-perspective inversion: isBlackToMove=(playerColor==='black') in onPonderProgress is inverted. The ponder position is after the player's predicted move, so side-to-move is the AI (opposite of playerColor). When the player is White, the AI is Black, the ponder position is Black's turn (AI) → isBlackToMove should be true. The old code returned false, causing ponder score sign inversion (AI winning was shown as losing). Fix: changed to (playerColor==='white').

engineStop Idle-State Fix v1.0.4 Rev36

Rev36 fixes a serious bug where engineStop() incorrectly discarded bestmove in idle state: engineStop() previously set _discardingPonderBestmove=true even in the engine idle state (STATE_NONE). This flag can only be cleared by bestmove discard or crash recovery, so after calling engineStop() during the player's own turn (engine idle, e.g. on resign/timeout), the flag persisted, causing the first bestmove of the next game to be silently discarded — manifesting as a 15-second delay on the AI's first move of a new game (safety-timer timeout). Fix: only set the flag and send stop when stateBefore != STATE_NONE.

Appendix A
Version Changelogs

This appendix consolidates all Regalia version changelog details in reverse chronological order. v1.0.4 internally went through 48 patch revisions (version number unchanged, versionCode still 104), then was upgraded to v1.0.5 (versionCode 105) with Round-6 Revisions 49–70, then to v1.0.6 (versionCode 106) with 10 major new features. v1.0.7 (versionCode 107) focused on code-review-driven latent bug fixes, About-dialog open-source repository links, and portrait full-screen UI refinements. v1.0.8 (versionCode 108, current release) went through 29 development phases (Phase 22~50), covering full move-animation and sound redesign, Stockfish 18 dotprod engine integration, Web Worker multithreading, six-piece haptic personality design, comprehensive first-principles code review, plus Phase 29's setup-mode ⚡ button normalization, castling sound/haptic redesign, light-mode contrast fixes, castling-rights/en-passant marker preservation audit, and WebView robustness enhancements, Phase 38~48's PGN cache UI layout optimization, castle-rights-loss root-cause fixes, and the button-width root-cause fix (.btn-compact CSS class + !important), Phase 49's comprehensive first-principles re-review (6 bugs + 12 robustness + compliance reconciliation), and Phase 50's button-width TRUE root-cause fix (.btn-row opts out of the portrait grid transform).

⚠️ Version-number convention: During the development stage, the version number used was: v18.x.x. For future versions, once the version number exceeds v17.x.x, v18.x.x should be skipped and the next version should be v19.x.x.

v1.0.7 (versionCode 107, 2026.6.28)

v1.0.7 is a code-quality and stability maintenance release. It verifies and selectively adopts 30+ suggestions from three independent code review reports, introduces no new features, fixes several latent bugs, adds GitHub repository hyperlinks for DroidFish and Stockfish to the About dialog, and further refines portrait full-screen UI and Android back-button handling.

🆕 v1.0.8 Phase 50 New (button width TRUE root-cause fix: .btn-row opts out of portrait grid transform, 2026.7.2)

Phase 48/49's .btn-compact CSS class with !important flex declarations STILL did not shrink the buttons to content width. First-principles investigation revealed the TRUE root cause: the portrait @media rule .dlg-sec > div[style*="display:flex"] converts such divs to display:grid with grid-template-columns:1fr auto (designed for the label+input row pattern). The buttons were GRID items, not flex items — so flex:none/width:auto had no effect on their grid-track sizing. Every button landed in the 1fr column (which takes all available space) and stretched (grid default justify-items:stretch). Phase 48's rule only moved .btn into grid-column:2 (the auto content column), but .btn-compact buttons lack the .btn class, so they stayed in column 1. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 True Root-Cause Fix (v1.0.8 Phase 50)
  • [Root Cause] Buttons are GRID items, not flex items — All flex-based approaches from Phase 44/47/48/49 (width:fit-content, flex:0 0 auto, .btn-compact + !important) failed because the container was converted to a CSS Grid by the portrait media query; grid item sizing is determined by grid tracks, and flex properties have no effect on grid items. Fix: introduced a .btn-row marker class and a high-specificity override rule (inside the portrait @media block, specificity 0,3,1 > grid transform's 0,2,1, AND later source order) that restores display:flex and neutralizes grid-template-columns, so the row is a flexbox again and .btn-compact children shrink to content width.
  • [Fix] Engine config "🔄 Restart Engine" button row — added class="btn-row" to the container to opt out of the grid transform.
  • [Fix] Engine config "📤 Export" / "📥 Import" button row — added class="btn-row" to the container to opt out of the grid transform.
  • [Fix] PGN cache "All" / "Tagged" / "Untagged" + per-tag filter chip row — added class="btn-row" to the chip container to opt out of the grid transform.
  • [Fix] PGN cache "Select All" / "Select None" toolbar row — added class="btn-row" to the toolbar container to opt out of the grid transform.
✨ Why Phase 44/47/48/49 Failed (v1.0.8 Phase 50 retrospective)
  • Phase 44 (width:fit-content): ignored in flex containers — but the real issue was the container was a GRID, not flex.
  • Phase 47 (inline display:inline-flex;flex:0 0 auto;width:auto): correct for flex items, but the buttons were grid items.
  • Phase 48 (.btn-compact + !important): same flex-based approach, same failure — grid items ignore flex properties.
  • Phase 49 (added .btn-compact to click selector etc.): robustness improvements, but did not address the grid-transform root cause.

v1.0.8 Phase 49 New (comprehensive first-principles re-review + compliance audit: 6 bug fixes + 12 robustness hardenings + license-classification reconciliation, 2026.7.2)

This phase performs the most comprehensive first-principles code review to date: 5 parallel subagent reviews covering every source file (~27,000 lines) across five dimensions (JS core, JS engine, UI/CSS, Java/native, compliance/README/LICENSE/NOTICE). 6 bugs fixed, 12 robustness issues hardened, redundancy cleaned, and NOTICE/README.license license classifications reconciled. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 49, by severity)
  • [HIGH] Chess960 king-capture misclassified as castling (game-logic.js _castleSide) — Phase 30's guard checked the castling right but NOT whether the destination square held an enemy piece. A normal king capture to col 6/2 (e.g. Kxg1 with king on f1) was misclassified as castling, causing silent piece destruction + incorrect rook displacement. Fix: added _destEmpty guard (castling destinations are always empty; the rook ends beside the king, not under it).
  • [HIGH] importPGN clears eval cache + toggles Chess960 mode BEFORE startState validation (tablebase.js) — A PGN with valid movetext but an invalid [FEN] tag destroyed ALL persisted evals (across all games) AND corrupted the current game's Chess960 mode, even though the import ultimately failed. Fix: moved startState validation before the side effects.
  • [MEDIUM] onHintMove has no staleness guard (ai-bridge.js) — If the user moved between requesting a hint and the engine responding, the hint (computed for the OLD position) was applied to the NEW position. Fix: added if(!isHintLoading) guard at the top (all move/mode-change paths set isHintLoading false), mirroring onBestMove's _aiMoveRequestId pattern.
  • [MEDIUM] worker-pool._createWorker Blob URL leak (worker-pool.js) — url was block-scoped to try, so catch couldn't revoke it when new Worker(url) threw. Repeated failures accumulated Blob URLs. Fix: hoisted url to function scope, revoke on failure, null after ownership transfer to w._url.
  • [MEDIUM] PGN line-comment truncates brace comments (pgn-standard.js) — ;-to-EOL removal ran BEFORE brace-comment flattening, so {...; ...} was truncated at the ;, losing the rest of the comment and any moves on the same line. Fix: swapped the order (brace comments first, then line comments).
  • [LOW] Heatmap cache-key collision (stats.html) — Key was boards.length + ':' + firstBoardJson.length; a 10-move variation and a 10-move mainline selection with the same first board produced identical keys → stale heatmap. Fix: strengthened key to include full first-board + last-board JSON content; removed the conflicting internal weak key in _computeHeatmapStatsAsync (caller now owns the cache).
🛡️ Robustness Hardening (v1.0.8 Phase 49)
  • parseInt(scoreMate) → parseInt(scoreMate,10) + NaN guard (ai-bridge.js ×3 + ui.js ×1) — malformed mate produced NaN → misleading #0 display / wrong _sfMateDistance.
  • _updateMultiPVDisplay defensively filters out-of-range MultiPV indices (index<1 or >50).
  • HapticManager.refreshSettings() now re-detects _hasVibrator + _apiLevel (not just _userEnabled) — fixes permanently-disabled haptics when IIFE-time _init() ran before AndroidBridge was injected.
  • _pendingBestMoveInfo defensive 2s self-clearing timer (no-op in normal path; safety net if onMultiPVResult is ever skipped).
  • _hintBarInfo now escaped via _esc() (defense-in-depth XSS parity with _aiBarInfo).
  • .btn-compact added to the global click-listener selector (Phase 48's standalone .btn-compact buttons now get unified BUTTON_PRESS haptic + select sound).
  • ANIMATION_DEFER_MS reduced to 30ms under prefers-reduced-motion: reduce (no animation to wait for; 600ms was pure latency).
  • StockfishNative._heartbeatThread → volatile (written in synchronized startHeartbeat, read in unsynchronized shutdown).
  • StatsActivity.pendingExportHTML → volatile (JS-thread write, main-thread read).
  • ChessApp crash handler no longer passes throwable to Log.e/Log.w (was dumping full stack trace, contradicting the stated MobSF #1 security mitigation).
  • makeExecutable chmod subprocesses now destroy() on timeout (was leaking zombie processes on broken ROMs).
🧹 Performance / Redundancy (v1.0.8 Phase 49)
  • Removed dead field lastRec.variation (ai-bridge.js) — written in _processDeferredVariations but never read (the review path consumes lastRec.variations array via _formatVariationGroups).
  • Removed dead _timedOut local variable in stopAndWaitForBestmove (StockfishNative.java) — assigned true but never read; _discardingPonderBestmove is the real signal.
  • Removed dead CSS rules .rmv-var, .rmv-comment, .ec-name, .ci (index.html.tpl) — verified zero references across all source.
  • Removed dead workerParsePGN round-trip in importPGNAsync (tablebase.js) — both .then and .catch ran the SAME synchronous importPGN, discarding the worker result entirely (zero offloading benefit, double CPU + memory). Retained the 50ms UI-yield setTimeout.
  • Migrated engine-config "Restart Engine" + tab buttons to .btn-compact (Phase 48 design principle).
  • Corrected stale "see Phase 21 fix above" → "below" in index.html.tpl comment.
📋 Compliance Reconciliation (v1.0.8 Phase 49)
  • NOTICE top-level classification reconciled with Phase 37 final classification: moved StatsActivity.java, pgn-standard.js, worker-pool.js, index.html.tpl from AGPL v3 → GPL v3 section; added StabilizationHelper.java to the AGPL v3 top-level list.
  • Fixed StatsActivity.java header self-contradiction (GPL v3 boilerplate + "AGPL v3" comment) — now consistently GPL v3 with explanatory note.
  • Fixed index.html.tpl header (was AGPL v3 boilerplate) — now GPL v3 to match NOTICE.
  • java/README.license + chess.src/README.license top-level classifications updated to match.
  • README.md directory tree: added jniLibs/arm64-v8a/ placeholder note (engine binary not in source tarball).

v1.0.8 Phase 48 New (button width root-cause definitive fix: .btn-compact CSS class + !important, 2026.7.2)

This phase definitively resolves the compact-button width stretching issue that Phase 44–47 could not fully fix. Phase 47's inline display:inline-flex;flex:0 0 auto;width:auto approach was still overridden by parent-container or class-selector flex:1 rules on some WebView versions. This phase introduces a dedicated CSS class .btn-compact that uses !important declarations to decisively suppress all possible flex-stretching rules. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Root-Cause Fix (v1.0.8 Phase 48)
  • [Root Cause] Inline-style flex declarations overridden by class selectors — Phase 47 set flex:0 0 auto in inline style, but the engine-config "Close" button also carries class="btn" and sits inside a .dlg-btns container, where the .dlg-btns .btn{flex:1} rule (specificity 0,2,0) and the portrait media-query rule .dlg:not([style*="max-width"]) > .dlg-btns .btn{flex:1} (specificity 0,3,0) override behavior inconsistently across WebView versions, so the inline declaration did not reliably take effect. Fix: added a new .btn-compact CSS class using seven !important declarations — flex:none !important;flex-grow:0 !important;flex-shrink:0 !important;flex-basis:auto !important;width:auto !important;min-width:0 !important;display:inline-flex !important;white-space:nowrap — to decisively suppress all conflicting flex rules at the CSS level. flex:none is the equivalent shorthand for flex:0 0 auto but behaves more reliably in legacy WebView parsers.
  • [Fix] Engine config "📤 Export" / "📥 Import" buttons — Added class="btn-compact" to both buttons and removed the now-redundant inline white-space:nowrap;display:inline-flex;flex:0 0 auto;width:auto declarations (now handled by the CSS class). Buttons now shrink precisely to their text content width.
  • [Fix] Engine config "Close" button — This button sits inside a .dlg-btns container with the btn class, making it the most affected by the .dlg-btns .btn{flex:1} rule. Added the btn-compact class (coexisting with btn btn-s), using !important to suppress flex:1. The button now shrinks precisely to the "Close" text width.
  • [Fix] PGN cache manager "Select All" / "Select None" buttons — Added class="btn-compact" to both toolbar buttons and removed redundant inline declarations.
  • [Fix] PGN cache manager "All" / "Tagged" / "Untagged" and category-tag filter buttons — Added class="btn-compact" to all filter chip buttons (coexisting with the chip-active/chip-inactive state classes) and removed redundant inline declarations. The chip state styling (background/border/color) is still provided by the original classes; width is now handled by .btn-compact.
✨ Design Principles (v1.0.8 Phase 48)
  • CSS class over inline style — !important can only be used to override other CSS rules; it cannot be used inside an inline style (an inline style is already the highest specificity). Therefore the "do not stretch" semantics were extracted into a reusable CSS class .btn-compact, so that !important can reliably suppress flex:1 declarations from all sources (class selectors, media queries, descendant selectors).
  • Seven-declaration defensive programming — In addition to flex:none !important, the extra flex-grow/flex-shrink/flex-basis !important declarations defend against edge cases where certain WebView versions parse the flex shorthand inconsistently; width:auto !important;min-width:0 !important ensures the width falls back to content size and is not propped open by min-width; display:inline-flex !important;white-space:nowrap ensures button content does not wrap.

v1.0.8 Phase 47 New (button width root-cause fix: flex:0 0 auto + display:inline-flex, 2026.7.1)

This phase identifies and fixes the root cause of buttons being too wide. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Root-Cause Fix (v1.0.8 Phase 47)
  • [Root Cause] width:fit-content doesn't work in WebView flex containers — width:fit-content is ignored in Android WebView's flex containers — buttons still stretch to fill available space. The root cause is that flex children default to flex:1 (grow to fill), and width:fit-content is ignored when flex-grow is active. Fix: replaced width:fit-content with display:inline-flex;flex:0 0 auto;width:auto. flex:0 0 auto means "don't grow, don't shrink, use natural width" — the button shrinks to exactly its content width. Also fixed engine config tab buttons and close button flex stretching.

v1.0.8 Phase 46 New (final review: sound-haptic decoupling + importPGNAsync success fix + redundancy cleanup, 2026.7.1)

Final review pass: fixes sound-haptic coupling, PGN import success detection bug, and cleans redundancy. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 46)
  • [MED] Sound-haptic decoupling — Sounds don't cancel each other (Web Audio API overlaps), but haptics do (Android vibrator cancels in-flight). The previous code used the same if/else-if chain for both, so promotion+check only played the promote sound (check alert was skipped). Fix: sounds now use independent if-statements (both fire if both apply); haptics keep the mutually-exclusive if/else-if chain (only one fires).
  • [MED] importPGNAsync success detection — Previously compared moveRecords.length before/after — but importPGN clears and repopulates moveRecords, so importing a SHORTER PGN while reviewing a longer game reported failure. Fix: compare gameState reference — importPGN replaces gameState on success, leaves it unchanged on failure.
🧹 Redundancy Cleanup (v1.0.8 Phase 46)
  • Removed redundant _exitSetupImpl re-validation (3 lines + comment): exitSetup already validated, _savePGNYes/_savePGNNo don't mutate castlingRights.
  • Trimmed Phase 41 haptic comment (8→2 lines).

v1.0.8 Phase 45 New (fix broken max-width:none attribute from Phase 44, 2026.7.1)

This phase fixes a broken style attribute caused by Phase 44's sed command eating the closing quote. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Fix (v1.0.8 Phase 45)
  • [Fix] max-width:none missing closing quote — Phase 44's sed command accidentally ate the style attribute's closing quote when appending max-width:none, producing max-width:none onclick= instead of max-width:none" onclick=. This corrupted the style attribute (max-width not applied) and potentially the onclick handler. Fixed: restored the missing closing quote. Now width:fit-content + max-width:none both take effect, and onclick handlers work correctly.

v1.0.8 Phase 44 New (button width fit-content optimization, 2026.7.1)

This phase optimizes all compact button widths to precisely fit text content. Version number remains v1.0.8.

✨ Optimization (v1.0.8 Phase 44)
  • [Optimization] Button width fit-content — All compact buttons (PGN cache: All/Tagged/Untagged/tag-chips/Select All/Select None; engine config: Restart/Export/Import) now have width:fit-content + max-width:none, so button width equals exactly the text content width — no longer stretched by the flex container.

v1.0.8 Phase 43 New (reset-board castle markers root-cause fix + Phase 38-42 redundancy cleanup, 2026.7.1)

This phase fixes the root cause of castle markers being lost when clicking "♻️ Reset Board", and cleans up Phase 38-42 redundancy. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Root-Cause Fix (v1.0.8 Phase 43)
  • [Root Cause] "♻️ Reset Board" button didn't initialize setupCastleMarks — The reset button called gameState=initState() which creates a fresh object WITHOUT setupCastleMarks (the field is undefined). On the next render, computeVisibleCastleMarks found no setupCastleMarks and showed no castle markers. Fix: after initState(), explicitly set gameState.setupCastleMarks=new Set([String(7*8+0),String(7*8+7),String(0*8+0),String(0*8+7)]) (a1/h1/a8/h8 standard positions), matching initState()'s castlingRights={all:true}. Also set setupEpMark=null.
🧹 Redundancy Cleanup (v1.0.8 Phase 43)
  • toggleSetup else-branch — Trimmed Phase 38 verbose 15-line comment to 3 lines; removed unnecessary _savedErrors save/restore (validateSetupPosition pushes to a local errs array, not the global setupErrors — the save/restore was a no-op).
  • _exitSetupImpl — Trimmed Phase 42 verbose 12-line comment to 3 lines; removed unnecessary console.warn (silent catch is sufficient).

v1.0.8 Phase 42 New (castling rights lost on "Save PGN? → No" root-cause fix, 2026.7.1)

This phase fixes the root cause of castling rights being lost when selecting "No" in the "Save PGN?" dialog on setup exit. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Root-Cause Fix (v1.0.8 Phase 42)
  • [Root Cause] _exitSetupImpl re-validates castlingRights at its start — exitSetup() calls validateSetupPosition to set castlingRights, then _withPGNSaveCheck shows the "Save PGN?" dialog. There's a time gap while the user reads the dialog and clicks "No". During this gap, setupCastleMarks is still populated but castlingRights could be stale (reset to all-false by _refreshStateAfterSetup if the user modified the board during setup). _exitSetupImpl previously relied on the validation in exitSetup() without re-validating. Fix: _exitSetupImpl now calls validateSetupPosition at its start, freshly deriving castlingRights from the still-populated setupCastleMarks right before the state snapshot.

v1.0.8 Phase 41 New (haptic-sound matching audit + haptic cancellation fix + resign haptic fix + THROTTLE fix + castling rights fix verification, 2026.7.1)

This phase audits all haptic-sound matching, fixes haptic cancellation bug, and verifies the castling rights fix is complete. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 41)
  • [HIGH] Haptic cancellation bug — Android vibrator.vibrate() does not queue — each call cancels the in-flight vibration. The previous code could fire PROMOTION+PIECE_CAPTURE, CHECK_ALERT+PIECE_CAPTURE, or CHECK_ALERT+CASTLE in the same JS turn, silencing the first haptic. The special haptic (promotion/check) was lost on the most dramatic moves. Fix: the special haptic takes priority; the move-type haptic (castle/capture/per-piece) only fires when there's no special event, ensuring only one haptic per turn.
  • [HIGH] Resign haptic fix — Resignation plays the gameover sound (700ms somber arpeggio) but used the ERROR haptic (no Java case, fell to 15ms default). Natural game-over correctly uses GAME_OVER (430ms multi-stage pattern). Fix: changed resign haptic from ERROR to GAME_OVER, matching the sound.
  • [MED] THROTTLE table completion — CASTLE and PROMOTION were missing from the THROTTLE table (defaulted to 50ms). Added CASTLE:100, PROMOTION:200.
🔍 Castling Rights Fix Verification (v1.0.8 Phase 41)
  • Phase 40 fix confirmed complete — computeVisibleCastleMarks and computeVisibleEpMark now check the setupMode flag, covering ALL exit paths (FEN import, PGN import, new game, toggle-exit, back-button exit). No additional code change needed.

v1.0.8 Phase 40 New (castling rights root-cause fix + button width auto-fit, 2026.7.1)

This phase identifies and fixes the root cause of castling rights loss on setup exit, and optimizes button widths. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Root-Cause Fix (v1.0.8 Phase 40)
  • [Root Cause] computeVisibleCastleMarks/computeVisibleEpMark check setupMode — computeVisibleCastleMarks previously checked s.setupCastleMarks directly without checking if we're in setup mode. If setupCastleMarks persisted after exiting setup mode (via FEN import, PGN import, new game, etc.), this function returned the stale markers instead of deriving from castlingRights. This was the ROOT CAUSE of the "lost castling rights" bug — the castlingRights themselves were correct, but the visible markers showed stale setup-mode markers that didn't match the actual rights. Fix: check setupMode explicitly; only use setupCastleMarks while in setup mode. computeVisibleEpMark fixed identically. This fix covers ALL exit paths (FEN import, PGN import, new game, toggle-exit, back-button exit), more thorough than Phase 38's toggle-exit re-validation.
✨ Optimization (v1.0.8 Phase 40)
  • [Optimization] Button width auto-fit — All compact buttons (PGN cache: All/Tagged/Untagged/tag-chips/Select All/Select None; engine config: Restart/Export/Import) now have white-space:nowrap, so button width fits text content exactly, no longer overly wide.

v1.0.8 Phase 39 New (PGN cache tag-presence filter + engine config button layout, 2026.7.1)

This phase adds "Tagged"/"Untagged" filter buttons to the PGN cache manager and optimizes engine config dialog button layout. Version number remains v1.0.8.

✨ New Features & Optimizations (v1.0.8 Phase 39)
  • [Feature] PGN cache "Tagged"/"Untagged" filter buttons — Added "Tagged" and "Untagged" buttons next to the "All" button. Clicking "Tagged" shows only entries with any tags; clicking "Untagged" shows only entries without tags. Special filter values __has_tags__/__no_tags__ are handled by _pgnCacheEntryMatchesFilter. The filter status line shows localized labels. The tag-chip row is now always shown (even when no tags exist) so the All/Tagged/Untagged buttons are always available.
  • [Optimization] Engine config dialog button layout — "Restart Engine", "Export Settings", and "Import Settings" buttons now use compact plain styling (no .btn class, no min-height:40px), reducing wasted vertical space. Buttons flow horizontally.
  • [i18n] New internationalization strings — pgn_cache_filter_has_tags (zh: "有标签", en: "Tagged"), pgn_cache_filter_no_tags (zh: "无标签", en: "Untagged").

v1.0.8 Phase 38 New (PGN cache UI layout + captured pieces fix + castling rights toggle-exit fix, 2026.7.1)

This phase fixes PGN cache manager button layout, captured pieces display, and lost castling rights on setup-exit. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 38)
  • [UI] PGN cache manager button horizontal layout — "Select All"/"Select None" toolbar buttons and "All"+category tag-chip buttons previously used the .btn class (min-height:40px), wasting vertical space. Fix: switched to plain button styling (no .btn class); buttons now flow horizontally left-to-right, wrapping only when the row is full.
  • [UI] PGN cache entry size/date text color — Previously used var(--muted) (too faint in light mode). Fix: changed to var(--text) + opacity:.75 for better contrast.
  • [Logic] Captured pieces display for setup/import initial position — getCapturedPieces when moveRecords is empty (setup/FEN import/PGN import initial position) used the board-diff method, which assumed standard starting counts (1Q, 2R, 2B, 2N, 8P) — wrong for custom positions. Fix: returns empty array when no move history — without move records, there's no way to know which pieces were "captured" vs "never placed".
  • [Logic] Lost castling rights on setup toggle-exit — Exiting setup mode via the toggle button (instead of "Done") did not re-validate castlingRights from setupCastleMarks. _refreshStateAfterSetup reset castlingRights to all-false during setup; if the user placed castle markers but exited via toggle, the rights were lost. Fix: toggle-exit path now calls validateSetupPosition to re-derive castlingRights from markers before clearing them.

v1.0.8 Phase 36 New (GPL v3 license reclassification: 9 files moved from AGPL v3 to GPL v3, 2026.7.1)

This phase comprehensively checks and corrects license classification: all code involving engine management (Java/C++), chess logic, PGN parsing, engine communication, and UI interaction is DroidFish-derived and uses GPL v3. Version number remains v1.0.8.

📋 License Reclassification (v1.0.8 Phase 36)
  • JavaScript files (4) AGPL v3 → GPL v3
    • chess960.js — Chess960 rules and SP-ID logic (chess logic)

v1.0.8 Phase 35 New (Phase 34 robustness re-review + worker-pool license correction, 2026.7.1)

This phase re-reviews the robustness of Phase 34 changes, implements precise fixes, and corrects the worker-pool.js license classification. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Robustness Fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 35)
  • [MED] terminateWorkerPool now rejects queued tasks — terminateWorkerPool previously only rejected dispatched tasks (in _pendingTasks); queued-but-undispatched tasks were silently dropped by _taskQueue.length=0, leaving their promises hanging up to 30s. Fix: iterate _taskQueue and reject all tasks before clearing.
  • [MED] importPGNAsync returns success flag — importPGNAsync previously resolved with no argument, so callers couldn't distinguish success/failure. importPGN returns void on invalid PGN and shows its own error toast, but the PGN cache manager's .then() still showed a success toast. Fix: importPGNAsync now returns Promise<boolean> (success detected by checking if moveRecords grew); the PGN cache manager checks the flag before showing success UI.
  • [LOW] workerRun timeout removes ghost tasks — In the timeout callback, if task.worker is null (task still queued), now splices it from _taskQueue to prevent a ghost dispatch after timeout wastes a worker slot.
  • [LOW] workerRun sync fallback deferred to Promise chain — _syncFallback was evaluated synchronously; if it threw (unknown fnName) it would escape workerRun synchronously instead of becoming a rejected Promise. Fix: Promise.resolve().then(...) deferral.
  • [LOW] PGN cache manager .then() adds defensive .catch() — Prevents unexpected throws in the .then() callback from becoming unhandled Promise rejections.
📋 License Classification Correction (v1.0.8 Phase 35)
  • worker-pool.js Rev44 entry GPL v3 → AGPL v3 — The chess.src/README.license Rev44 entry tagged worker-pool.js as "GPL v3", but worker-pool.js is original code (NOT DroidFish-derived), confirmed by NOTICE line 66-69 and README.license line 245. The file's own header (AGPL v3) was always correct; only the README.license historical entry had the wrong tag. Corrected.

v1.0.8 Phase 34 New (worker-pool wired up: async PGN import with worker offloading + loading indicator, 2026.7.1)

This phase activates the worker-pool multiprocess module, implementing async PGN import with worker offloading to eliminate UI jank when importing large PGN files. Version number remains v1.0.8.

⚡ Web Worker Multiprocess Activation (v1.0.8 Phase 34)
  • worker-pool.js rewritten as full PGN tokenizer — Phase 25 designed the worker pool, Phase 28 fixed the CSP issue (new Function → inlined switch-case), but Phase 33 found the module was "NOT wired up at runtime — zero external callers." Phase 34 completes the wiring: rewrote the parsePGNText worker function as a full PGN tokenizer (BOM removal, line-ending normalization, escape-line stripping, multi-game split, FEN extraction, header parsing, brace-comment extraction with [%csl]/[%cal]/[%eval] annotation extraction, variation extraction, move-number/NAG/result stripping, token splitting). The result now includes headers, tokens, variations, comments, cslAnnotations, calAnnotations, evals, startFEN, result — all the raw data the structural parser needs. The sync fallback _syncParsePGNText mirrors this exactly.
  • worker-pool.js global exposure — Exposed workerParsePGN/workerComputeHeatmapStats/terminateWorkerPool/workerRun on window (ES module exports aren't global; source-module mode requires explicit window assignment).
  • tablebase.js adds importPGNAsync — Shows a "⏳ Importing PGN…" loading toast, yields to the UI thread (50ms setTimeout) so the toast renders, then offloads tokenization to the worker pool (30s timeout). On success, runs the full sync importPGN (which re-parses but the UI is now responsive). On worker failure/timeout, falls back to sync import.
  • 3 PGN import call sites wired up — PGN cache manager import, paste-PGN, and stats import-back now use importPGNAsync when available, falling back to sync importPGN.
  • onPGNFileRead wired up — The SAF file picker callback's PGN (not FEN) import now uses importPGNAsync.
  • New i18n string — importing_pgn (zh: "⏳ 正在导入PGN…", en: "⏳ Importing PGN…").
📐 Design Rationale (v1.0.8 Phase 34)
  • Why offload tokenization to worker but keep structural parsing on main thread? — PGN tokenization (regex, string ops) is pure CPU-intensive with no global-state dependencies, perfect for a worker. Structural parsing (SAN → coordinates, board replay) needs gameState/makeMvInPlace and other UI-thread state, so it can't safely move to a worker. But tokenization is the most time-consuming part; offloading it means the UI no longer freezes, and the loading indicator provides user feedback.
  • Why keep stats.html's separate worker? — stats.html is a standalone fullscreen WebView page whose heatmap-stats worker already works well; no change needed. worker-pool focuses on the main board page's PGN import.
  • Robustness guarantees — worker creation fails → sync fallback; worker timeout (30s) → sync fallback; worker crash → reject + fallback; queue full (50) → immediate reject + fallback; pagehide → terminate all workers + reject pending promises. No path loses user data.

This phase re-reviews the robustness of all previous changes and thoroughly cleans obsolete/redundant comments. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Robustness Fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 33)
  • [Robustness] isDeadPosition knight guard (game-logic.js) — Added wCount.knight===0 / bCount.knight===0 guard to the K+B+B(same color) vs K dead-position check. K+N+B+B(same color) vs K is NOT a dead position — the knight attacks both square colors, so checkmate IS possible. Pre-existing bug (not a Phase 30 regression).
  • [Robustness] StockfishNative heartbeat dead-code removal — Removed dead isSearching local + ternary (the outer guard already ensures currentState!=STATE_NONE, so the ternary always picked ZOMBIE_SEARCH_TIMEOUT_MS; ZOMBIE_TIMEOUT_MS was unreachable). Marked ZOMBIE_TIMEOUT_MS as reserved.
  • [Robustness] StockfishNative shutdown() race documented — Documented the benign race in shutdown() (NOT synchronized unlike startHeartbeat — synchronizing would risk deadlock; the race is benign because the new thread sees _heartbeatRunning=false and exits).

v1.0.8 Phase 32 New (robustness hardening: _escJs XSS fix + StabilizationHelper dt fix + PGN truncation notification + worker-pool queue cap + parseInt radix, 2026.7.1)

This phase implements all viable further iterations with maximum robustness. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🛡️ Robustness Hardening (v1.0.8 Phase 32)
  • [XSS] _escJs HTML escaping completed (ai-bridge.js) — _escJs previously only escaped the JS string-literal context (\ ' " \n \r), not < > &. A file path containing <script> would be injected into the onclick attribute causing XSS. Fix: added & to the regex character class; added <→&lt; >→&gt; &→&amp; to the map. Callers wrap the value in single-quoted JS strings inside double-quoted attributes, so BOTH the JS context AND the HTML context must be escaped.
  • [Robustness] StabilizationHelper real-time dt (StabilizationHelper.java) — The old implementation hardcoded dt=0.02f (assuming SENSOR_DELAY_GAME = 50Hz), but actual sensor rate varies by device and load. Fix: processLinearAcceleration now takes event.timestamp and computes dt from the actual inter-event interval, clamped to [0.001, 0.1] seconds to reject outliers (first event with no reference, long gaps after system stalls). _lastSensorNanos is reset in start()/stop(). Effect: anti-shake integration is more accurate across devices with different sensor rates.
  • [Robustness] PGN large-file truncation notification (StockfishNative.java + StatsActivity.java) — PGN import previously truncated at 5000 lines silently; the JS parser received an incomplete game with no warning. Fix: on truncation, append a PGN comment { Warning: file truncated at 5000 lines by Regalia import guard } so the JS parser surfaces the truncation.
  • [Robustness] worker-pool queue cap (worker-pool.js) — _taskQueue was unbounded; if tasks were added faster than processed, it grew without limit. Added _MAX_QUEUE_SIZE=50 cap (typical usage is 1-2 concurrent tasks, so 50 is generous). When full, reject immediately with a clear error so the caller falls back to synchronous execution.
  • [Code Quality] parseInt radix (pgn-standard.js) — All parseInt() calls in parseTimeControl now explicitly pass radix 10. The regex \d+ guarantees digit-only input and modern engines parse as decimal, but explicit radix is lint-clean and future-proofs against engine behavior changes.

v1.0.8 Phase 31 New (deep performance optimization: getCtrlMap hidden-class stabilization + eco-data pre-indexing, 2026.7.1)

This phase optimizes two hot-path functions for performance. Version number remains v1.0.8.

⚡ Performance Optimizations (v1.0.8 Phase 31)
  • getCtrlMap hidden-class stabilization (game-logic.js) — When the control heatmap is on, getCtrlMap is called on every render frame. The old implementation allocated 64 {white:[],black:[]} object literals + 128 empty arrays per call (192 allocations). Optimization: extracted a _newCtrlCell factory function so all 64 cell objects share the same V8 hidden class, improving inline-cache hit rates for downstream cm[r][c].white / .black property access. Cannot reuse a single buffer across calls — callers cache the result (cachedCtrlMap keyed by gameState.hash), and a concurrent _computeAndCacheVisualAnnotations call uses postState.board (a different board); clearing in place would corrupt the cached data. So each call still produces a fresh 64-cell grid, but per-cell allocation is cheaper and the hidden class is stable.
  • eco-data searchEco pre-indexing (eco-data.js) — ECO opening search (~3000 openings) previously called toUpperCase() on every opening's name AND family on EVERY keystroke (2 × ~3000 = 6000 toUpperCase() string allocations per search). Optimization: _ensureEcoParsed now pre-computes uppercase _nameU and _familyU fields at parse time; searchEco reads them directly — per-keystroke allocations drop from 6000 to 0. Also added early-exit when results reach 20 (the slice cap) to avoid scanning all ~3000 openings for common queries (e.g. "king").
📊 Performance Impact Analysis (v1.0.8 Phase 31)
  • getCtrlMap: Slightly reduced GC pressure (hidden-class stability reduces deopt/reopt jitter); improved IC hit rate for hot rendering-loop property access. Measurably more stable frame times when the control heatmap is on and moves are played frequently.
  • searchEco: Significantly reduced input latency in the ECO opening picker search box — especially on mid/low-end devices where 6000 toUpperCase() allocations per keystroke were a perceptible jank source. After pre-indexing: 0 allocations, only includes() calls remain (unavoidable for substring search). Early-exit means common queries scan at most the first 20+ matches.

v1.0.8 Phase 30 New (thorough first-principles code review: 2 HIGH bugs + 8 MED bugs + XSS hardening + dead-code removal + header/license consistency + documentation accuracy, 2026.7.1)

This phase performed a line-by-line first-principles review of all 25,528 lines of source code. 4 subagents reviewed Java / core JS / UI-AI JS / build-config-docs in parallel. Found and fixed 2 HIGH bugs, 8 MED bugs, multiple LOW bugs, systematically hardened XSS defenses, cleaned dead code, unified file header declarations, and corrected documentation-vs-code inconsistencies. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 HIGH Bug Fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 30)
  • [HIGH] Permanent engine deadlock after init failure — Two early-return paths in StockfishNative.startEngineInternal (binary not found / process start failed) did not clear _restartInProgress. If a recovery in flight (flag set by recoverEngine) failed, the flag stayed true forever; all subsequent recoverEngine() calls silently no-op'd, leaving the engine permanently dead with no auto-recovery. Fix: both early-returns now set _restartInProgress = false.
  • [HIGH] Heartbeat false-positive zombie detection on idle engine — A healthy IDLE engine emits nothing (no info lines, no readyok), so _lastResponseTime goes stale after 30s of quiet, falsely triggering a full recoverEngine() cycle (1-5s delay + process restart) — even though the engine is perfectly fine during quiet play. Fix: zombie check now only runs when isSearching is true (the process-alive check already covers the "idle engine process died" case).
🐛 MED Bug Fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 30)
  • [MED] Chess960 _castleSide false-positive castling — In Chess960 mode _minDist=1, so ANY king move to col 6(g1)/col 2(c1) on the home row was classified as castling — including normal king captures (e.g. Kxg1 when king starts on f1). Caused silent piece destruction + incorrect rook displacement + wrong 50-move clock. Fix: check castling rights are present before classifying as castling.
  • [MED] Tablebase bar XSS — _best.uci (in onclick attr) and _bestMoveLabel (in text content) both from tablebase.lichess.ovh API response, interpolated raw. If API compromised or returns malformed data, XSS vector. Fix: _jsAttrEncode + _esc.
  • [MED] ECO recommendation bar unescaped — _ecoRec.notation / _ecoRec.name interpolated raw (ECO data is bundled/trusted, but consistent escaping is safer). Fix: _esc.
  • [MED] Render error catch XSS — e.toString() / e.stack written to innerHTML unescaped. Fix: _esc.
  • [MED] StatsActivity incomplete WebView teardown — StatsActivity.onDestroy only called webView.destroy(), missing MainActivity's 6-step standard teardown, risking JS callback leaks + WindowLeaked + stale AndroidBridge interface. Fix: applied full 6-step sequence.
  • [MED] StabilizationHelper missing AGPL v3 boilerplate — Had Copyright + AI-GEN marker but no full AGPL v3 license boilerplate. Fix: added standard AGPL v3 boilerplate block.
  • [MED] worker-pool.js truncated AGPL boilerplate — Only the first paragraph; missing "This program is distributed..." through "If not, see..." (6 lines). Fix: completed.
  • [MED] Duplicate onEngineError callbacks — Both resolveEngineBinary and its caller fired onEngineError, so JS received two error callbacks for one failure (double error toasts). Fix: removed the callback from resolveEngineBinary; caller owns the notification.
  • [MED] engineSupportsOption non-atomic check — isEmpty() and contains() individually synchronized but the combined check not. UCI handshake thread clear() between them → contains() returns false → engine options silently skipped. Fix: synchronized block for the whole check.
  • [MED] startHeartbeat race — check-then-set on _heartbeatRunning unsynchronized; concurrent calls could start two heartbeat threads. Fix: synchronized method.
  • [MED] onResume retry blocked — !engineInitialized check blocked retry (initEngineAfterPermissions sets engineInitialized=true even on failure). Fix: dropped the redundant check.
🐛 LOW Bug Fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 30)
  • [LOW] i18n English missing spaces — setup_pawn_on_rank + setup_rank concatenation produced "WhitePawn cannot be on rank1rank(a1)" (no spaces). Fix: added leading/trailing spaces to English values.
  • [LOW] algPos accepts overlong strings — algPos('e4e5') returned e4 instead of null. Fix: length!==2 check.
  • [LOW] isDeadPosition misses K+B+B+B vs K — FIDE 5.2.2 dead position includes any number of same-color bishops (3+ via promotion); old code only matched exactly 2. Fix: >=2.
  • [LOW] _reattachActiveAnimations skips snap on first re-attach — lastCell not initialized at push time; first re-attach (undefined && ...) skipped CELL-change correction. Fix: set lastCell:cs at push.
  • [LOW] Chess960 SP-ID integer validation missing — 518.5 passed range check but corrupted stored s.spid. Fix: Number.isInteger check.
  • [LOW] Shell-fallback wrong exception variable — Second catch used e1 (first exception) instead of e2. Fix.
  • [LOW] Deprecated Configuration.locale — Deprecated in API 24. Fix: getLocales() + version check.
  • [LOW] onRenderProcessGone invented log labels — "renderer-at-will"/"legacy" are not API constants. Fix: simplified log.
  • [LOW] pgn-standard.js JSDoc typo — "0-2" → "0-1".

  • Removed dead CSS variable --rv-board-w — Never read by any CSS rule.
