v1.0.8 Phase 29 New (setup-mode ⚡ button normalization + castling sound/haptic redesign + light-mode contrast fixes + castling-rights/en-passant marker preservation audit + WebView robustness enhancements, 2026.7.1)

This phase addresses 5 user-reported issues and systematically enhances WebView robustness, based on user feedback and five WebView development guide PDFs (Android WebView Application Development Specification Guide, WebView Performance & Robustness Optimization Guide, Android Light Theme Design Principles, Android Dark Theme Design Principles, Advanced WebView Development Guide) using first-principles verification. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🎯 User-feedback fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 29)
  • [Setup-mode ⚡ button normalization] — The "⚡" button on the setup-mode button bar (en-passant marker toggle) was previously forced to text-mode rendering by the .setup-btn class's font-variant-emoji:text, rendering ⚡ as a monochrome text glyph (black/white lines), inconsistent with the colorful emoji ⚡ fixed on the board in Phase 26. Fix: added inline style font-variant-emoji:emoji;-webkit-font-variant-emoji:emoji to the ⚡ button, forcing standard colorful emoji rendering, visually consistent with the on-board ⚡ marker. The 🔁 button keeps text mode (🔁 U+1F501 has no emoji glyph under Noto Sans).
  • [Castling sound redesign] — The castling sound (playCastleRookMove) was originally a soft 200→350Hz triangle-wave rising tone (250ms), lacking the decisiveness and power befitting a royal maneuver. Redesigned as a two-stage "snap + slam" rapid sound (135ms): Stage 1 (0-45ms) low-frequency impact (110Hz sine thump + 1800Hz bandpass noise crack); Stage 2 (45-135ms) metallic crash (220→80Hz sawtooth down-sweep + 2500Hz highpass noise shimmer). Paired with a synchronized haptic redesign.
  • [Castling haptic matched] — The CASTLE haptic pattern (StockfishNative.java) was originally a gentle double-tap (40-30-50ms, amplitudes 160/50/200, total 120ms). Redesigned as a two-stage intense vibration synchronized with the sound (total 105ms): Stage 1 (0-35ms) sharp intense snap (amplitude 255, max); 10ms gap; Stage 2 (45-105ms) heavy rumble slam (amplitude 220). API 35+ PWLE and API 26+ waveform dual-path coverage. Conveys "majestic rapidity" — the king commands, the rook instantly obeys with a heavy thud.
  • [Light-mode setup-error contrast fix] — The "⚠️ Cannot complete setup" notification's per-reason text color was too faint in light mode. Root cause: .setup-errors color was hardcoded to #f5a0a0 (a dark-mode-specific pink; on the light #f0f0f3 background its contrast ratio was only 1.8:1, far below WCAG AA's 4.5:1). Fix: .setup-errors, .setup-errors strong, and .setup-errors li now all use var(--setup-err-color); light-mode --setup-err-color deepened from #c0392b to #a02818 (contrast ratio 5.4:1, meets AA).
  • [PGN cache search-box light-mode fix] — The PGN cache manager's "Search name or tags…" placeholder was too faint in light mode. Root cause: the search box's background was hardcoded to rgba(42,21,32,.6) (dark-mode-specific translucent dark-red) and border to rgba(212,160,23,.3) (dark-mode-specific gold); in light mode the background was near-black and the placeholder inherited the browser-default 50%-opacity --text, yielding insufficient contrast. Fix: background now uses var(--input-bg), border uses var(--border); added a new --placeholder theme variable (dark #c0a070 warm gray, light #4a4a52 deep slate), applied globally via ::placeholder, ::-webkit-input-placeholder, and :-ms-input-placeholder rules with opacity:1 so the variable value is used verbatim.
🔍 Castling-rights / en-passant marker preservation audit (v1.0.8 Phase 29)
  • End-to-end data-flow verification — Audited whether castling-rights and en-passant markers are correctly preserved when completing setup. Verified chain: (1) On entering setup mode, setupCastleMarks is seeded from castlingRights, setupEpMark is seeded from enPassantTarget (converting SKIPPED square → PAWN square); (2) During setup, _refreshStateAfterSetup resets castlingRights/enPassantTarget on every board mutation but preserves setupCastleMarks/setupEpMark; (3) On completing setup, _validateSetupCastleMarks/_validateSetupEpMark re-derive castlingRights/enPassantTarget, syncHash recomputes the Zobrist hash; (4) _exitSetupImpl generates _setupFEN, clears transient marker fields, deep-clones via cloneS into stateHistory/reviewBaseState; (5) In play mode, computeVisibleCastleMarks/computeVisibleEpMark derive visible markers from castlingRights/enPassantTarget. Conclusion: preservation logic is correct; round-trip is lossless.
  • Defensive assertion added — Added a defensive check before the snapshot in _exitSetupImpl: if castlingRights is missing or wrong type, restore the all-false default; if enPassantTarget is present but malformed (non-object, non-numeric row/col, out of bounds), clear it to null. Guards against future regressions in _validateSetupCastleMarks/_validateSetupEpMark leaving the state half-mutated and causing a crash.
🛡️ WebView robustness enhancements (v1.0.8 Phase 29, first-principles per PDF guides)
  • [Safe Browsing enabled] — WebSettings.setSafeBrowsingEnabled(true) (API 26+). Although the app only loads local file:///android_asset/ resources, as defense-in-depth Safe Browsing checks any unexpected navigation (meta refresh, JS window.open, etc.) against Google's malware/phishing blocklist. Per: WebView Performance & Robustness Optimization Guide §Security configuration.
  • [Render-process crash handling] — ChessWebViewClient added onRenderProcessGone callback (API 26+). The WebView renderer runs in a separate process; on OOM/GPU fault/native crash this callback fires. Old behavior: WebView left in a dead black-screen state, user had to force-kill the app. Fix: destroy the dead WebView (remove from parent to avoid WindowLeaked), rebuild Activity+WebView via activity.recreate() (engine subprocess is independent and persists; SharedPreferences/PGN cache persist). Returns true to tell the framework we handled it, so the app process isn't killed. Per: WebView Performance & Robustness Optimization Guide §Robustness §2. Crash prevention.
  • [WebView destroy sequence completed] — MainActivity.onDestroy's WebView destroy was originally just webView.destroy(). Per the PDF standard destroy sequence, expanded to 6 steps: (1) removeView to prevent WindowLeaked; (2) clearHistory to release navigation history; (3) loadUrl("about:blank") to clear the document + JS callbacks; (4) removeJavascriptInterface("AndroidBridge") to unregister the JS interface; (5) onPause to pause JS timers; (6) destroy for native teardown. Each step is independently try/caught so a single step failure doesn't block subsequent steps. Per: WebView Performance & Robustness Optimization Guide §Robustness §1. Standard destroy sequence.
🎨 Theme system enhancements (v1.0.8 Phase 29)
  • New --placeholder theme variable — Dark mode #c0a070 (warm gray), light mode #4a4a52 (deep slate). Applied globally via ::placeholder rule with opacity:1 so the variable value is used verbatim (no longer subject to the browser's default 50%-opacity hack). All input placeholders now meet WCAG AA 4.5:1 contrast in both modes.
  • Error color deepened — Light-mode --setup-err-color deepened from #c0392b to #a02818 (contrast 5.4:1); dark mode brightened from #e74c3c to #ff6b5a (more salient on dark background).

v1.0.8 Phase 28 New (comprehensive first-principles re-review: 8 bug fixes + haptic fallback fix + Worker CSP fix + heatmap cache fix + castle/promotion haptic, 2026.7.1)

This phase performs another thorough first-principles code review. 3 subagents reviewed all source files (26,534 lines) in parallel, finding and fixing 8 bugs + redundancy cleanup. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Bug fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 28, by severity)
  • [HIGH] _reattachActiveAnimations double bug — _fc/_fr were const-scoped inside the if-block, causing a ReferenceError in the snap-to-dest path (silently caught by try/catch); and the snap formula _fc*cs+a.dx*(cs/a.lastCell) double-counted the source offset (left/top already positions at source, transform should be just scaled dx/dy). Effect: orientation change mid-animation snapped the overlay to the SOURCE square for up to 660ms. Fixed: moved _fc/_fr to loop top; transform = just a.dx*(cs/a.lastCell).
  • [HIGH] validateSetupPosition pawn-rank formula swapped — Phase 24's fix had the ternary backwards: (r===0)?1:8 should be (r===0)?8:1 (row 0 = rank 8 = black's back rank, row 7 = rank 1 = white's back rank). Produced self-contradictory errors like "Pawn cannot be on rank 1 (a8)". Fixed.
  • [HIGH] _checkPVDivergence Chess960 castling field name wrong — Phase 24's fix used mr.castle (the move-object field name), but move records use mr.isCastling (boolean). mr.castle was always undefined, so Phase 24's fix never triggered — every Chess960 castling move in a PV continuation still caused a false divergence. Fixed: mr.castle → mr.isCastling.
  • [MEDIUM] Chess960 PGN [FEN] tag corruption (Phase 24 fix overridden) — Phase 24 set the correct starting FEN in startFEN, but subsequent code overwrote supObj.FEN with generateFEN(gameState) (the current mid-game state). Corrupted the [FEN] tag for any progressed game. Fixed: removed the overwrite; only convert castling-rights to Shredder format on the starting FEN.
  • [MEDIUM] stats.html html[data-theme="dark"] incomplete — Only set color-scheme:dark without re-declaring the full dark palette. When system is light but JS forces dark (Xiaomi HyperOS 3), the stats page showed light variables. Fixed: restore the full dark palette (mirrors :root).
  • [MEDIUM] Heatmap cache not invalidated on new PGN import — Switching between same-length standard-chess games showed stale heatmap stats from the previous game. Fixed: clear _heatmapCacheKey/_heatmapCacheResult in _statsPastePGN and onStatsPGNFileRead.
  • [MEDIUM] tryPwleVibrate fallback lost multi-stage pattern — When PWLE reflection failed on API 35+, the internal fallback created a single OneShot (e.g. queen's 390ms single buzz), losing the case statement's multi-stage waveform. Fixed: tryPwleVibrate returns boolean; on failure the case statement falls through to the API 26+ waveform branch (preserving the multi-stage pattern).
  • [LOW] Landscape .review-hdr override stripped safe-area — The landscape media-query padding override removed the env(safe-area-inset-top) that Phase 26 added. Fixed: landscape override preserves safe-area-top.
  • [LOW] Review eval error catch called wrong function — engineEvalDeep synchronous failure called _updateEvalDisplay() (updates the hidden main eval bar) instead of _updateAllEvalDisplays(). The visible #review-eval-bar stayed stuck at "Analyzing". Fixed.
🐛 Haptic fallback fix + Castle/Promotion haptic (v1.0.8 Phase 28)
  • tryPwleVibrate fallback fix — As above, PWLE failure no longer degrades to a single OneShot; it falls through to the case statement's multi-stage waveform. All haptic patterns (pawn/knight/bishop/rook/queen/king/castle/promotion/check/game-over) correctly show multi-stage patterns on PWLE-unavailable devices.
  • CASTLE haptic added — New CASTLE case (double-tap: king step + rook slide); previously castling fell to the 15ms default (less tactile than a normal move). API 35+ PWLE + API 26+ waveform + legacy fallback.
  • PROMOTION haptic added — New PROMOTION case (celebratory ascending triad: three rising pulses); previously promotion had no celebratory haptic.
🐛 Worker CSP fix + memory leak fix (v1.0.8 Phase 28)
  • worker-pool.js CSP incompatibility — Phase 25's implementation used new Function() to inject function source into the worker, which requires CSP script-src 'unsafe-eval' — the app CSP does NOT allow this. Fixed: inlined the function logic directly into the worker source string (switch-case dispatch), no dynamic evaluation needed.
  • stats.html worker onerror memory leak — _statsWorker.onerror nulled the worker without calling .terminate() or URL.revokeObjectURL(). Fixed: added terminate + revokeObjectURL.
  • worker-pool.js timed-out tasks not removed from queue — Timed-out tasks were removed from _pendingTasks but stayed in _taskQueue, permanently marking the worker busy when their result arrived. Fixed: remove from queue only when dispatched.
  • worker-pool.js terminateWorkerPool didn't clean pending — Didn't clear pending timeouts or reject promises. Fixed: clear timeouts + reject all pending promises.
🧹 Redundancy cleanup (v1.0.8 Phase 28)
  • Removed dead variable ponderFen — ai-bridge.js onBestMove had const ponderFen=generateFEN(gameState) computed but never used (only ponderFenAfterMove was passed to startPonder). Removed, saving one generateFEN call per AI move.

v1.0.8 Phase 27 New (knight/bishop/rook dedicated haptic feedback — all six pieces now have personality-matched haptics, 2026.7.1)

This phase designs dedicated haptic feedback for the knight, bishop, and rook, complementing their respective move animations and sound effects. All six piece types (pawn/knight/bishop/rook/queen/king) now have dedicated haptic feedback. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🎨 Knight/Bishop/Rook dedicated haptic design (v1.0.8 Phase 27)
  • Knight · agile jump + crisp landing — Haptic: KNIGHT_MOVE. Design: a gentle lift-off ramp (30ms ramp-up) → brief mid-air gap (40ms low amplitude) → sharp crisp landing peak (25ms high-amplitude sharp tick). Matches the knight's L-shape parabolic jump animation + crisp "ding" landing sound. API 35+ uses PWLE waveform ([0, 0.35, 0.1, 0.7, 0]), API 26+ uses waveform fallback, lower APIs use fallbackVibrate(60ms).
  • Bishop · sharp smooth glide — Haptic: BISHOP_MOVE. Design: a single smooth bell-curve swell (40ms ramp-up → 50ms peak → 40ms ramp-down), no hard peak — the bishop slides swiftly and cleanly along the diagonal. Matches the bishop's sawtooth-glide + filter-sweep sound (270ms). API 35+ PWLE ([0, 0.4, 0.45, 0.2, 0]), API 26+ waveform fallback, lower API fallbackVibrate(70ms).
  • Rook · fierce charge-dash-impact — Haptic: ROOK_MOVE. Design: low charge rumble (25ms medium amplitude) → dash gap (35ms low amplitude) → heavy impact thud (60ms full-amplitude slam) → aftershock (25+40ms decay). Matches the rook's 3-stage sound (charge low-freq + dash whoosh + heavy impact) + light board shake. API 35+ PWLE ([0, 0.5, 0.15, 0.85, 0.3, 0.5, 0]), API 26+ waveform fallback, lower API fallbackVibrate(120ms).
  • Haptic personality spectrum — Pawn (shivering · 3 tiny ticks) < Bishop (sharp glide · smooth bell) < Knight (agile jump · lift-off + crisp landing) < Rook (fierce charge + impact) < Queen (resounding · massive slam) < King (solemn · 4 measured thuds). Amplitude and duration increase, reflecting the light-to-heavy personality spectrum of the pieces.
  • Implementation — executeMove (ui.js) haptic dispatch simplified to piece.type.toUpperCase()+'_MOVE', uniformly covering all six pieces. HapticManager (ai-bridge.js) THROTTLE table gains KNIGHT_MOVE:45, BISHOP_MOVE:40, ROOK_MOVE:50. StockfishNative.performHapticInternal() (Java) gains three new cases, each with API 35+ PWLE / API 26+ waveform / legacy fallback.

v1.0.8 Phase 26 New (personified animation/sound/haptic upgrade + notch adaptation + shake/anti-shake coexistence + landscape board shrink + ⚡emoji fix + stats dialog light-mode + Worker race fix, 2026.7.1)

This phase addresses multiple user-reported visual/audio/haptic/compatibility/race-condition issues via first-principles fixes and optimizations. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🎨 Personified animation/sound/haptic upgrade (v1.0.8 Phase 26)
  • Pawn · shivering — Animation: high-frequency low-amplitude tremor (22 keyframes, tremor amplitude = 1.8% of cell, 14 alternations), non-linear progress (hesitate→drift→settle), scale < 1.0 throughout (feather-light), soft expand to 1.0 on landing. Sound: three quick wavering squeaks (frequency jitter) + soft landing. Haptic: PAWN_MOVE — three tiny vibrations (API 35+ PWLE waveform). Duration 260ms.
  • Queen · resounding/ground-shaking — Animation: heavier than rook (520ms), large scale swell mid-flight (1.12), pre-landing compression to 0.92 then snap to 1.18 ("clanking" wind-up-slam), triggers massive shake (shake-massive, 620ms, ±6px, heavier than king's heavy). Sound: low brass growl + metallic clang + massive impact. Haptic: QUEEN_MOVE — massive impact waveform. Duration 520ms.
  • King · regal/majestic — Animation: more solemn than rook (560ms, longest), four measured steps (smooth bell curve, depth = 2.5% of cell), subtle scale breath (1.0→1.02→1.0), triggers heavy shake. Sound: deeper bell partials (90Hz fundamental) + four deeper footsteps (80Hz). Haptic: KING_MOVE — four measured thuds. Duration 560ms.
  • Smoothness guarantee — All keyframes mutate ONLY transform (GPU-composited pure transform), no per-frame filter/box-shadow changes, sustaining high fps. ANIMATION_DEFER_MS changed from 560 to 600 (matches the new longest animation + shake duration).
📱 Notch/cutout/R-corner adaptation (v1.0.8 Phase 26)
  • Review header — .review-hdr now uses padding:calc(14px + env(safe-area-inset-top)) ..., so the header is no longer obscured by notches/cutouts. .review-overlay covers the full viewport (inset:0), so the header must reserve space for the status bar/notch.
🐛 Shake vs anti-shake coexistence fix (v1.0.8 Phase 26)
  • Root cause — StabilizationHelper applies a CSS transform to .bwrap.stabilized for sensor-based translation compensation. When _triggerBoardShake adds the .shake-* class, the shake animation's transform overrides the anti-shake transform, causing a visual jump — both fight over the same transform property.
  • Fix — _triggerBoardShake removes the .stabilized class (pauses anti-shake) before adding .shake-*. After the shake ends, .stabilized is naturally restored by the next sensor event (~20ms). Eliminates the conflict.
🐛 Landscape board shrink fix (v1.0.8 Phase 26)
  • Problem — In landscape mode with anti-shake active, the board's right edge was clipped by .main's overflow-x:hidden when anti-shake shifted it rightward by 8px.
  • Fix — Anti-shake reservation increased from 8px to 12px (8px max displacement + 4px buffer), slightly shrinking the landscape board so the right edge is never clipped when anti-shake is active.
🐛 ⚡ marker emoji fix (v1.0.8 Phase 26)
  • Root cause — .setup-ep-mark was forced to text mode (font-variant-emoji:text) + purple color:var(--setup-ep-mark) (#9b59b6), causing ⚡ to render as a wrong-colored purple glyph instead of the proper yellow/orange emoji lightning bolt.
  • Fix — Removed font-variant-emoji:text and color, letting ⚡ render as a standard color emoji. The outline is preserved via text-shadow (which works on color emoji) instead of -webkit-text-stroke (which does NOT work on color emoji — it's ignored by the emoji renderer). The outline stays ultra-thin dark (0.3px rgba(0,0,0,.85) equivalent). 🔁 (castle-rights marker) keeps text-mode + color + stroke (it's not an emoji).
🐛 Stats export/import dialog light-mode fix (v1.0.8 Phase 26)
  • Problem — The stats page's export-HTML dialog and import-PGN dialog used hardcoded dark backgrounds (#221015) and gold borders (#d4a017), inconsistent with the silver palette in light mode.
  • Fix — All three dialogs' background changed to var(--card), border to var(--border), title color to var(--accent2), added color:var(--text).
🐛 Web Worker race-condition fix (v1.0.8 Phase 26)
  • Root cause — The stats.html heatmap worker overwrote w.onmessage on every call. If two calls overlapped (rapid re-render), the first call's onmessage was replaced by the second's, and the first call's Promise never resolved (memory leak + stuck loading placeholder).
  • Fix — Uses a taskId map so each concurrent call gets its own resolution. The worker echoes taskId in its response. onerror rejects all pending tasks.

v1.0.8 Phase 25 New (robust Web Worker multi-threading + portrait review chart height fix + ↹Global toggle fix + stats header light-mode fix, 2026.7.1)

This phase addresses 4 user-reported issues via first-principles fixes: worker-pool.js's design intent (use Web Worker multi-threading to avoid UI jank) was not realized, the portrait review eval chart was too tall (squeezing the move list), the "↹Global" toggle had a visual glitch, and the stats page header background didn't adapt to light mode. Version number remains v1.0.8.

⚡ Robust Web Worker multi-threading (v1.0.8 Phase 25, first-principles)
  • Design intent — worker-pool.js's original intent was to use Web Worker multi-threading to offload heavy computations (PGN parsing, heatmap-stats walk, control-map computation) to background threads, avoiding UI jank. Phase 24 deleted the never-called dead-code worker-pool.js (581 lines). This phase reimplements and correctly wires it in.
  • First-principles analysis — The most robust implementation must satisfy: (1) self-contained worker source (Workers can't access the main thread's scope, all logic must be inlined); (2) graceful degradation (fall back to synchronous execution if Worker creation fails — callers don't need to know); (3) task cancellation + timeout (stuck workers are terminated and replaced); (4) pool recycling (avoid per-task worker create/destroy overhead).
  • Implementation — Recreated worker-pool.js with: a pool of N workers (N = min(hardwareConcurrency, 4)), Blob-URL workers (CSP already allows worker-src blob:), a generic "run named function" protocol (extensible to new task types without regenerating workers), 30s task timeout + worker termination/replacement, pagehide auto-cleanup to prevent zombie workers.
  • Wiring: stats.html heatmap stats — The stats page's heatmap-control walk (1-2s for 100+ move games) is the biggest UI-jank source. stats.html now uses an inline Web Worker (self-contained _STATS_WORKER_SRC) to compute per-square control counts in a background thread; the main thread renders from the cached result. First render (cache miss) shows a loading placeholder; the worker computes in the background and triggers a re-render when done. CSP gains worker-src blob: and script-src blob:. Falls back to synchronous computation (_computeHeatmapStatsSync) if Worker is unavailable.
  • Wiring: chess.html PGN text parsing — worker-pool.js provides workerParsePGN and workerComputeHeatmapStats convenience functions, and is back in the build-chess.py module order (game-logic → chess960 → pgn-standard → worker-pool → ai-bridge → tablebase → eco-data → ui, 8 modules).
  • Not wired: getCtrlMap — The main-app getCtrlMap (called during render) stays synchronous. First-principles analysis: render() needs the control map immediately for rendering; async would introduce flicker. Also getCtrlMap is already cached by cachedCtrlKey (per-position hash), so the amortized per-render cost is low — it's not the main UI-jank cause.
🐛 Portrait review eval chart height fix (v1.0.8 Phase 25)
  • Problem — In portrait mode, the review eval trend chart was too tall (up to 200px), squeezing the move list's available space and showing too few move rows.
  • Fix — Portrait chart height changed from Math.max(120, Math.min(200, innerHeight-140)) to Math.max(100, Math.min(120, Math.floor((innerHeight-200)*0.18))). Portrait max reduced to 120px (was 200px), min 100px (was 120px). The freed space goes to the move list. Landscape height unchanged (120-200px).
🐛 "↹Global" toggle appearance fix (v1.0.8 Phase 25, first-principles)
  • First-principles root-cause analysis — The "↹Global" toggle above the review eval chart had an abnormal appearance. Root cause: the .toggle-sw CSS class uses an ::after pseudo-element to render the dot (16px dot, left:1px/19px). But the previous HTML code created a custom inline <div> dot inside .toggle-sw (12px dot, left:1px/13px, hardcoded background). This caused two dots to render simultaneously — one from CSS ::after (correct theme color), one from the inline <div> (hardcoded var(--bg)/var(--accent2), overlapping and offset from ::after).
  • Fix — Removed the inline <div> dot; use the standard .toggle-sw + ::after CSS. Also added a .toggle-sw.sm variant class (30x16 switch + 12px dot + left:1px/17px) for compact toolbars (review header, chart global toggle, move-history card). Previously these small switches used inline style="width:30px;height:16px" overrides, but the ::after dot was still 16px (on a 30px switch, on-state left:19px → 19+16=35 > 30, dot overflowed). The .sm variant correctly scales the dot and travel.
🐛 Stats page header light-mode fix (v1.0.8 Phase 25)
  • Problem — The .hdr section at the top of the stats page (containing the title and buttons like "💾HTML") didn't adapt to light mode. .hdr used a hardcoded background:linear-gradient(145deg,#2a1a0a,#1a0a0a) (dark brown gradient); in light mode, when the rest of the page turned silver, the header stayed dark brown — visually inconsistent.
  • Fix — .hdr background changed to linear-gradient(145deg,var(--hdr-bg),var(--bg)), using a new --hdr-bg theme variable. --hdr-bg is defined in :root (dark: #1a0a0a), @media(prefers-color-scheme:light) (light: #f0f0f3), and html[data-theme="light"] (JS-driven light: #f0f0f3). Dark mode keeps the deep brown gradient; light mode gets a silver gradient consistent with the page.

🐛 Bug fixes (v1.0.8 Phase 24, by severity)
  • [HIGH] stats.html XSS vulnerability — PGN header values inserted into the metadata table unescaped; a malicious PGN (e.g. [White "<script>..."]) would execute on the stats page. Fixed by wrapping with _escFEN().
  • [MEDIUM] Chess960 PGN [FEN] tag corruption — _setupFEN was null for Chess960 games started from the New Game dialog, causing _buildPGNString to fall back to generateFEN(gameState) (the CURRENT mid-game state) — corrupt PGN export. Fixed by setting _setupFEN at Chess960 game start.
  • [MEDIUM] Eval bar showed pre-move eval during animation — executeMove didn't call _resetEvalState() before _updateEvalDisplay(), leaving the bar showing the old eval during the 560ms animation window. Fixed.
  • [MEDIUM] _resetGameUIState ghost pieces — set animationInProgress=false but didn't clear _activeAnimEls or remove overlay DOM — _reattachActiveAnimations() re-attached stale overlays. Fixed to call _clearAnimationState().
  • [MEDIUM] flipBoard/enterReview/exitReview/toggleSetup animation state not cleared — these 4 functions didn't call _clearAnimationState() when invoked during the ~520ms animation window, leaving overlays with wrong orientation/state. Fixed (all 4 now call it).
  • [MEDIUM] StockfishNative.recoverEngine executor leak — each recovery cycle created a new ExecutorService without shutting down the old one, leaking non-daemon threads. Fixed with _engineExecutor.shutdown() before creating a fresh one.
  • [MEDIUM] StockfishNative.makeExecutable chmod mismatch — fallback used chmod 755 but nativeChmod sets 0744. Fixed to 744.
  • [MEDIUM] EngineService.isRunning non-volatile — read from JS binder thread and service main thread. Fixed to volatile.
  • [MEDIUM] MainActivity.onActivityResult cancel not handled — early return on user-cancel left _pendingExportContent stale, hanging "Exporting..." dialogs forever. Fixed with cancelPendingExport().
  • [MEDIUM] index.html.tpl html[data-theme="dark"] incomplete — only overrode 7 chart variables; when system was light but JS forced dark, the page rendered light with dark chart colors. Fixed to restore the FULL dark palette.
  • [LOW] Chess960 _checkPVDivergence false-positive on castling — _mrToUci returns "e1g1" (king actual) but pvMoves holds "e1h1" (king captures rook), triggering false divergence on every Chess960 castling move. Fixed to skip the divergence check for castling moves in Chess960 mode.
  • [LOW] _triggerBoardShake didn't clear stale _cachedBwrap — Fixed.
  • [LOW] AndroidBridge.isEngineReady() without typeof guard — 9 call sites across game-logic.js, ai-bridge.js, ui.js. All fixed.
  • [LOW] validateSetupPosition incomplete pawn-rank check — only checked one rank per color with swapped rank-number literals in error messages. Fixed to check both rank 1 and rank 8.
  • [LOW] _reattachActiveAnimations didn't recompute dx/dy on CELL change — orientation change mid-animation landed the overlay on the wrong square. Fixed to cancel the WAAPI animation and snap to the new destination.
  • [LOW] stats.html viewport blocked zoom — maximum-scale=1.0, user-scalable=no violates WCAG 1.4.4. Fixed to maximum-scale=5.0, user-scalable=yes.
  • [LOW] stats.html title hardcoded Chinese — Fixed to "📊Statistics".
  • [LOW] stats.html target="_blank" without rel — tab-nabbing risk. Fixed with rel="noopener noreferrer".
  • [LOW] stats.html NaN% on division by zero — time-per-phase distribution showed NaN% when total thinking time was 0. Fixed with total>0 guard.
  • [LOW] i18n 'book' English translation wrong — was 'Mediocre', should be 'Book'. Fixed.
  • [LOW] chess960.js comment had swapped bishop file sets — light bishop files commented as {0,2,4,6} (actually dark), dark as {1,3,5,7} (actually light). Fixed.

v1.0.8 Phase 23 New (⚡ marker rendering root-cause fix + first-principles optimization of post-move flicker & animation smoothness + Stockfish 18 dotprod engine + comprehensive code review, 2026.7.1)

This phase addresses two visual issues reported by the user — the ⚡ (en-passant marker) on the main board rendering abnormally, and pieces flickering after the move animation completes — through first-principles root-cause analysis and fixes. It also downloads and integrates the official Stockfish 18 arm64-v8a-dotprod engine binary (replacing the previous generic arm64-v8a build, enabling DOTPROD instruction acceleration), and performs a thorough first-principles review of all source code. Version number remains v1.0.8.

🐛 Main-board ⚡ marker abnormal rendering root-cause fix (v1.0.8 Phase 23)
  • Root-cause analysis — The user reported that the ⚡ (en-passant marker) on the main board appeared as a blurry purple blob, while the review-board ⚡ rendered correctly (sharp). First-principles analysis:
    • Main-board squares use the .sq class, so the CSS rule .sq .setup-ep-mark matches and applies color:var(--setup-ep-mark) (purple #9b59b6) + text-shadow:0 0 2px rgba(0,0,0,.85),0 0 4px rgba(0,0,0,.55) (two-layer dark shadow) + filter:drop-shadow(0 0 1px rgba(255,255,255,.45)) (white glow). Three layered shadows over a purple ⚡ glyph produce a muddy/blurry visual on Android WebView (Xiaomi HyperOS 3) — this is the root cause of "main-board ⚡ abnormal".
    • Review-board squares do NOT have the .sq class (just <div style="position:relative">), so the .sq .setup-ep-mark selector does not match, and the review-board ⚡ falls back to the system's colorful emoji rendering (sharp yellow) — this is why "review-board ⚡ is normal".
  • Fix — Changed the CSS selector from .sq .setup-castle-mark, .sq .setup-ep-mark to .setup-castle-mark, .setup-ep-mark (removed the .sq ancestor requirement) so both boards share the same styling. Also:
    • Removed text-shadow (two-layer dark shadow) — eliminates the blur source
    • Removed filter:drop-shadow (white glow) — eliminates the compounded blur
    • Changed -webkit-text-stroke from .4px rgba(255,255,255,.85) (thick white stroke) to .3px rgba(0,0,0,.85) (ultra-thin dark stroke), per the user's requirement of "ultra-thin dark outline"
    • Kept paint-order:stroke fill (stroke first, fill on top — stroke acts as outline)
  • Result — Both main-board and review-board ⚡ now render in text mode via font-variant-emoji:text (purple #9b59b6 dark / #6a2c8e light) with a 0.3px ultra-thin dark outline, crisp and clear on both light and dark squares. 🔁 (castle-rights marker) gets the same treatment (gold + ultra-thin dark outline) for visual consistency.
🐛 Post-move piece flicker root-cause fix (v1.0.8 Phase 23, first-principles)
  • Root-cause analysis (first-principles) — Pieces flickered abnormally after the move animation. The timing is:
    1. t=0: animateMove() is called; source piece opacity=0 (hidden); overlay (.move-anim) created and animation starts
    2. t=0..520ms: overlay animates from source to destination square
    3. t≈520ms: Web Animations API onfinish fires _finishAnim(), which immediately calls el.remove() to delete the overlay and sets animationInProgress=false
    4. t=560ms: executeMove's setTimeout(ANIMATION_DEFER_MS=560) callback fires requestAnimationFrame(updateAfterMove)
    5. t≈576ms: render() executes app.innerHTML=h to rebuild the DOM (with the new state, piece at destination)
    Problem: Between t=520ms (overlay deleted) and t=576ms (new DOM painted) there is a ~40–56ms visual gap — the source piece is still hidden (opacity=0), the overlay is gone, and the new DOM hasn't been built yet, so both the source and destination squares appear empty — perceived by the user as "piece flicker".
  • Fix (first-principles) — _finishAnim() no longer calls el.remove() / rookEl.remove(). The overlay stays visible at the destination square until render() runs app.innerHTML=h, which destroys the .bwrap subtree (including the overlay) and rebuilds it with the new state in a single synchronous DOM mutation. The browser paints the new state in the same frame — the visual gap is eliminated. _activeAnimEls is still cleared so _reattachActiveAnimations() won't re-append the now-stale overlay to the new DOM.
  • Stale-closure path keeps the remove — When _myGen !== _animGen (a newer animation started, current closure is stale), el.remove() is still called because the newer animateMove already cleaned up old overlays at its start; this is a belt-and-suspenders safety.
⚡ Animation smoothness breakthrough (v1.0.8 Phase 23, first-principles)
  • Root-cause analysis (first-principles) — Animation was not smooth. Analysis revealed that the knight/bishop/queen/king animation keyframes each set a different filter:drop-shadow(...) value:
    • Knight: 18 keyframes, each with filter:'drop-shadow(0 '+(arc*8)+'px '+(arc*6)+'px rgba(0,0,0,0.4))' (varying with parabolic arc)
    • Bishop: 5 keyframes, each with a different golden-glow drop-shadow
    • Queen: 16 keyframes, each with double drop-shadow (golden glow + dark shadow), values varying with sin(t*π)
    • King: 24 keyframes, each with drop-shadow(0 '+(6+sin(t*π)*3)+'px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.55))'
    filter:drop-shadow is a pixel-level operation (computes shadow shape from the alpha channel). Changing filter on every keyframe forces the browser to re-rasterize the alpha mask — even when the element is on a GPU composited layer (will-change:transform), filter changes still trigger pixel recomputation, causing frame drops.
  • Fix (first-principles) — Set filter:drop-shadow(0 4px 5px rgba(0,0,0,0.45)) as a static CSS property on the .move-anim class. When the overlay is created, the browser computes filter once (rasterizes the alpha mask + shadow) and caches the result as the composited layer's texture. During animation, each keyframe only changes transform (a pure GPU-composited layer translation, zero pixel ops); filter stays constant, and the texture is reused. All filter properties were removed from keyframes.
  • Visual trade-off — A static shadow means the shadow no longer grows/shrinks during the animation (e.g., the knight's shadow no longer "grows" during its jump). But the static shadow still provides depth, and for short 250–520ms animations the dynamic shadow's visual benefit is negligible while the smoothness gain is significant. This is the correct performance/visual trade-off.
🐛 Ghost-piece fix on undo/flip during animation (v1.0.8 Phase 23)
  • Root cause — _clearAnimationState() (called on undo/redo/flip) only set animationInProgress=false; it did not clear the _activeAnimEls array or remove leftover .move-anim overlay nodes from the DOM. When render() then called _reattachActiveAnimations(), that function saw _activeAnimEls non-empty and re-appended the stale overlay to the new DOM, showing a "ghost piece".
  • Fix — _clearAnimationState() now clears _activeAnimEls, bumps _animGen (so any in-flight _finishAnim closure self-invalidates), and proactively removes all .move-anim overlay nodes under .bwrap.
⚙️ Stockfish 18 arm64-v8a-dotprod engine integration (v1.0.8 Phase 23)
  • Official binary — Downloaded stockfish-android-armv8-dotprod.tar from the official GitHub release (Stockfish 18, sf_18 tag), extracted the stockfish-android-armv8-dotprod binary (114MB, ELF 64-bit ARM aarch64, statically linked, Android 29+, built with NDK r27c, stripped). Renamed to lib/arm64-v8a/libstockfish.so under jniLibs per Android packaging convention.
  • DOTPROD instruction acceleration — The dotprod variant enables ARMv8.6-A DOTPROD instructions (SDOT/UDOT) for integer matrix-multiply acceleration in neural-network inference. On modern ARM big cores (Cortex-A76/A77/A78/X1/X2/X3/X4 + Snapdragon 8-series/7-series Gen1+) it delivers significant inference speedup vs. the generic arm64-v8a build — shorter thinking time at the same depth.
  • Compatibility — The dotprod variant requires the CPU to support the ARMv8.6-A DOTPROD extension. Older devices without this instruction (e.g., Cortex-A53/A55/A72/A75) will crash at startup. minSdk=21 is unchanged, but actual runtime requires an ARMv8.6-A-compatible CPU (~mid-to-high-end devices from 2020 onward). All Xiaomi HyperOS 3 devices support it.

  • build.gradle — Removed the java { toolchain { languageVersion = JavaLanguageVersion.of(21) } } block (Gradle toolchain auto-detection is unavailable without the foojay plugin); now uses org.gradle.java.home in gradle.properties to specify the JDK directly.
  • APK signing — Verified v1/v2/v3 signing schemes are all enabled (enableV1Signing / enableV2Signing / enableV3Signing all true), compatible with Xiaomi HyperOS 3 install verification.

v1.0.8 Phase 22 New (Complete redesign of move animation & sound effects + light mode support, 2026.6.30)

This phase, following the "棋魂 · Personified Chess Move Animation" and "Personified Chess Sound Effects" reference documents, completely discards the v1.0.7 move animation and sound implementation (no old code or comments retained) and redesigns a personified animation and sound system. Light mode is also added following the "Android Dark Theme Design Principles" and "Android Light Theme Design Principles" — light/dark mode switches automatically with the system global setting.

🎨 Move Animation Redesign (v1.0.8 Phase 22)
  • Personified piece animations — Each piece has a unique personified motion characteristic, implemented via Web Animations API (el.animate()) + translate3d + will-change:transform for GPU-composited 120fps rendering:
    • ♙ Pawn (timid) — Hesitate-back then dart forward (scale 0.88 → 1.05 → 1.0), 250ms, cubic-bezier(0.25,0.05,0.25,1.15) slight overshoot easing.
    • ♘ Knight (agile) — L-shape parabolic jump (24-frame parabola, arc height = 28% of cell), with slight rotation (±4°) and dynamic drop-shadow, 380ms, cubic-bezier(0.34,1.42,0.64,1) bounce easing.
    • ♗ Bishop (sharp) — Quick diagonal glide with golden glow trail (drop-shadow 0→12px→0), 270ms, cubic-bezier(0.05,0.92,0.18,1) sharp easing.
    • ♖ Rook (fierce) — Charge-dash-impact with light board shake (.bwrap.shake-light, 280ms), 290ms, cubic-bezier(0.95,0.05,0.25,1) dash easing.
    • ♕ Queen (elegant) — Graceful arc (20-frame curve) with golden aura (drop-shadow 16px), 420ms, cubic-bezier(0.65,0,0.35,1) elegant easing.
    • ♔ King (solemn) — Heavy measured step (28-frame wobble, 4 micro-tremors per journey) with heavy board shake (.bwrap.shake-heavy, 450ms), 520ms, cubic-bezier(0.4,0,0.2,1) heavy easing.
  • Higher value → longer duration → heavier feel — Pawn 250ms < Bishop 270ms < Rook 290ms < Knight 380ms < Queen 420ms < King 520ms. Durations are 60% of the reference spec (reference is for demo mode; gameplay needs to stay responsive).
  • Board shake feedback — Rook and King landing triggers board shake (CSS keyframes .bwrap.shake-light / .shake-heavy), restarted via void offsetWidth forced reflow for rapid successive calls. Amplitude: light ±2px, heavy ±4px.
  • Castling compatibility — King and rook animate concurrently (preserving v1.0.7's synchronous approach; the reference's 3-stage narrative is too slow for gameplay). Chess960 _kingStayedPut case (king already on castling target) only animates the rook, skipping the king overlay.
  • prefers-reduced-motion support — JS-side detection of OS-level "Reduce Motion" setting; when matched, the entire animation path is skipped (no overlay, no shake), only sound is played. CSS @media(prefers-reduced-motion:reduce) also disables shake animations.
  • Generation counter race-condition guard — _animGen generation counter ensures stale _finishAnim closures cannot corrupt newer animation's global state (mechanism introduced in v1.0.7 Phase 18, retained).
  • DOM rebuild re-attach — _activeAnimEls tracks active overlay nodes; _reattachActiveAnimations() re-attaches them after render() rebuilds the .bwrap DOM, preventing mid-animation interruption.
🔊 Personified Sound Redesign (v1.0.8 Phase 22)
  • ChessAudioEngine sound engine — Pure Web Audio API synthesis (no external audio files), with each piece's timbre matching its personified animation personality:
    • ♙ Pawn (timid) — Triangle wave three-stage: 0ms hesitate squeak (380→340Hz), 80ms mid wood tap (420Hz), 160ms soft landing (280→170Hz sine).
    • ♘ Knight (agile) — Sine frequency sweep: 0ms rising whoosh (300→900→600Hz), 250ms crisp ding (1200Hz + 2400Hz overtone).
    • ♗ Bishop (sharp) — Sawtooth glide (500→1400→900Hz) + lowpass filter sweep (800→3000→1200Hz, Q=6).
    • ♖ Rook (fierce) — 0ms charge low-freq (80→60Hz square), 50ms dash whoosh (noise + bandpass 400→1500Hz), 250ms heavy impact (140→50Hz square + lowpass noise).
    • ♕ Queen (elegant) — Three-frequency harmony (220/330/440Hz sine) + 4.5Hz LFO vibrato + 60ms high overtone accent (880Hz).
    • ♔ King (solemn) — 0ms bell partials (110/220/330/440/550Hz, decreasing decay), 85ms four heavy footsteps (95→60Hz sine, synced with animation wobble).
  • Sound timeline aligned with animation — Sound key points precisely correspond to animation keyframe offsets (e.g., Knight's "ding" triggers at 250ms, matching the descent phase after the parabola peak).
  • Audio routing chain — master gain → [dry + reverb→reverbGain] → DynamicsCompressor → destination. Compressor threshold=-14dB prevents multi-voice clipping; convolution reverb (1.4s impulse) adds board spatial depth.
  • Mobile unlock — On first pointerdown/keydown, calls unlock() which plays a silent buffer to activate AudioContext (mobile browsers require user-gesture activation).
  • Node recycling — _activeNodes Set tracks all live oscillators; onended auto-cleans, preventing memory leaks. All exponentialRampToValueAtTime targets ≥ 0.0001 to avoid NaN.
  • Graceful degradation — If init() fails, all play* methods silently return without affecting animation flow. playSound(type) signature preserved; internally maps to the new engine ('move' → playPawn() as fallback; actual piece sounds are triggered by _playPieceSound inside animateMove based on piece type).
  • Sound toggle preserved — soundOn variable + toggleSound() function + toolbar button (🔊/🔇) unchanged. setEnabled() smoothly transitions volume via setTargetAtTime.
🎨 Light Mode Support (v1.0.8 Phase 22)
  • Light/dark mode follows system — Via CSS @media (prefers-color-scheme: light) media query, the app automatically switches light/dark mode following the system global theme setting, with no in-app manual toggle needed.
  • Continued elegant & solemn design — Light mode preserves the dark mode's "baroque chessboard" aesthetic: warm cream background (#f5ead6) + deep gold accent (#b8860b) + deep brown text (#3a2410), forming a harmonious "day/night" correspondence with the dark mode's warm brown-red + bright gold palette. The color system follows Material Design light theme principles (white/light-gray background, high-contrast dark text, moderately saturated brand color, WCAG AA 4.5:1 contrast).
  • CSS variable system — All key colors (background, card, border, text, accent, button, shadow, etc.) are defined via CSS variables; light mode only overrides variable values, and component styles adapt automatically. color-scheme: dark light declaration tells the browser both modes are supported, correctly rendering native UI like scrollbars and form controls.
  • Loading overlay king icon switch — The king icon on the engine initialization loading overlay (_loadingOverlay) switches based on system theme:
    • Dark mode: White king ♔ (silver-obsidian body #E8E8F0 + dark stroke + dark glow), identical to white pieces on the board.
    • Light mode: Black king ♚ (deep-obsidian body #1A1A2E + light gold stroke + light gold glow), identical to black pieces on the board.
    The outer gold gradient border (border-image: linear-gradient(145deg, #8b6914, #d4a017, #ffd700, #fff8dc, ...)) is unchanged in both modes; only the king symbol itself and its piece styling switch.
  • Main header toolbar king icon switch — The king icon on the left side of the main header toolbar (before the "Regalia" app name) also switches between ♔/♚ based on system theme, consistent with the loading overlay.
  • Stats page synchronized — The standalone stats.html statistics page also adds light mode support (:root + @media (prefers-color-scheme: light)), maintaining visual consistency with the main app.
🧹 Complete Removal of Old Code (v1.0.8 Phase 22)
  • game-logic.js old animation code removed — Deleted _lastAnimPieceType / _lastAnimTarget / _lastCaptureFlag / _lastCheckFlag / _landingAnimActive / _landingAnimTimer / _animFinishTimer / _startLandingTimer() / old animateMove() function body (170+ lines) and all other old animation state variables and functions. The new animateMove() preserves the original signature animateMove(from,to,pieceSym,pieceType,isCapture,isCheck,pieceColor).
  • ui.js old sound code removed — Deleted audioCtx / getAudioCtx() / old playSound(type) function body (7 sound types move/capture/check/castle/promote/gameover/hint with simple oscillator synthesis). The new playSound(type) preserves the signature and internally maps to the ChessAudioEngine. A new audioEngine global variable (ChessAudioEngine instance) is added for animateMove to trigger piece-specific sounds.
  • index.html.tpl old CSS animations removed — Deleted 6 landing keyframes (pawnStep / knightJump / bishopGlide / rookSlide / queenGlide / kingStep) + 6 .sq .pc.anim-* rules + captureFlash / captureCore keyframes + 6 .move-anim.anim-* transition rules. Added shakeLight / shakeHeavy keyframes for rook/king landing shake. Retained checkPulse / checkBgPulse (check king red glow pulse), castlePulse (castling rook marker gold pulse), gameOverFade / gameOverIcon / gtAnim (game-over overlay animations).
  • Cross-file reference adaptation — 13 places in ui.js that read old animation state (_lastAnimPieceType / _landingAnimActive / _startLandingTimer etc.) are all adapted: render throttle check simplified to only animationInProgress; landing animation class computation (animCls) entirely removed (new design uses Web Animations API overlay to cover the destination square, no CSS landing animation needed); cleanup code in _clearAnimationState() / _resetGameUIState() / _cleanupEventListeners() simplified accordingly.
  • HapticManager unchanged — The haptic feedback system (HapticManager 5-level degradation chain + AndroidBridge.performHaptic(type) Java vibration) is completely untouched; only sound was redesigned.
🐛 _srcRookPc Undefined Error + Piece Returns to Source After Animation + Move Highlight Fix (v1.0.8 Phase 22 eighth supplement)
  • _srcRookPc undefined error — Error _srcRookPc is not defined after move. Root cause: Previous fix referenced _srcRookPc in _finishAnim() to restore castling rook opacity, but _srcRookPc is a const local variable defined inside if(isCastling&&pieceColor) → if(rFromCol>=0&&rFromCol!==rToCol) nested block — when not castling or condition not met, the variable doesn't exist, causing ReferenceError. Fix: removed all manual opacity restoration code from _finishAnim().
  • Piece returns to source position after animation — After move animation, piece briefly returns to source position then jumps to target. Root cause: _finishAnim()'s manual opacity='' restoration acted on old DOM elements — but executeMove executes gameState=ns (new state) immediately after calling animateMove, and subsequent render() rebuilds DOM with new state. If _finishAnim executes after render(), opacity restoration targets stale DOM elements — the source-position piece (opacity restored to visible) briefly appears, causing the "returns to source" visual artifact. Fix: completely removed opacity restoration from _finishAnim(). The next render() rebuilds DOM with new state, naturally restoring all piece opacities to default (1) — no manual restoration needed.
  • Move highlight border rollback and correct fix — Previous round misdiagnosed the move highlight visibility issue, changing from box-shadow to outline. The actual cause was that light-mode CSS variable values needed to be synced. Fix: rolled back to box-shadow (inset 0 0 0 3px var(--last-to)), ensuring both dark mode --last-to:#8bc34a (bright yellow-green) and light mode --last-to:#689f38 (deep yellow-green) apply correctly. Added z-index:2 to ensure highlight is visible above pieces.
🐛 Castling Rights Loss + ⚡ Marker Abnormal + Animation Flicker + stats.html Light Mode Fix (v1.0.8 Phase 22 seventh supplement)
  • Castling rights abnormally lost after setup completion — validateSetupPosition() modified castlingRights and enPassantTarget but did not call syncHash(s) to re-sync the Zobrist hash. This caused gameState.hash to be stale, and subsequent cloneS copied the stale hash, with posCount Map entries based on the wrong hash — potentially causing castling-rights detection anomalies during state restoration. Fixed: added syncHash(s) at the end of validateSetupPosition().
  • Animation flicker at end of piece move — animateMove() set the source piece's opacity to '0' at animation start (overlay replaces it), but _finishAnim() only removed the overlay nodes without restoring the source piece's opacity. Between _finishAnim and the next render() call, the source piece remained invisible — causing flicker. Fixed: _finishAnim() now immediately restores opacity='' for source piece, captured piece, and castling rook, ensuring smooth transition.
  • stats.html not entering light mode with system — StatsActivity.java's anonymous AndroidBridge object did not include the isSystemDarkMode() method. stats.html's init() called AndroidBridge.isSystemDarkMode() which failed (method not found), falling back to matchMedia — unreliable on Xiaomi HyperOS 3. Fixed: added @JavascriptInterface isSystemDarkMode() method to StatsActivity's anonymous Bridge object, using the same UiModeManager detection logic as StockfishNative.
  • ℹ️ button lacking sound — The global click listener's closest() selector did not include .hdr-btn and .hdr-btn-lg classes, so clicking the ℹ️ button and language toggle did not trigger playSound('select'). Fixed: added .hdr-btn, .hdr-btn-lg to the selector list.
  • Last-move highlight yellow-green not implemented — .sq has contain:layout style paint; some WebView versions clip inset box-shadow, making the move highlight invisible. Fixed: changed move highlight from box-shadow to outline (unaffected by contain); box-shadow retained only for glow effect.
🎨 Comprehensive Light-Mode Polish + Move Highlight Color + Sound Supplement (v1.0.8 Phase 22 sixth supplement)
  • Move highlight color optimization — The last-move highlight box color was too low-saturation and not eye-catching. --last-to changed from #27ae60 (dark) / #1e7e34 (light) to vibrant yellow-green #8bc34a (dark) / #689f38 (light), glow increased from rgba(39,174,96,.06) to rgba(139,195,74,.15) (dark) / rgba(104,159,56,.12) (light), greatly improving visibility.
  • Comprehensive light-mode dark-color fix — 14 hardcoded dark backgrounds (#221015 / #1a0a0a / #2d1a22) replaced with CSS variables, covering: quick toolbar (.qtoolbar), AI hint bar (.hint-area), dialogs (.dlg), color buttons (.clr-btn), opening list buttons (.op-btn), promotion dialog (.prom-dlg / .prom-btn), setup panel (.setup-panel / .setup-btn / .setup-clr / .setup-del), move record blocks (.rmv-block), fullscreen dialog header/footer (.dlg > h2 / .dlg > .dlg-btns). All these elements now use the silver palette in light mode.
  • Toggle switch display fix — Global toggle switches displayed incorrectly in light mode when ON. Root cause: the switch dot (.toggle-sw::after) used var(--accent2) when OFF and var(--bg) when ON — in light mode, accent2 is dark and bg is light, but toggle-on-bg is also dark, causing insufficient contrast when ON. Fixed: added 3 new CSS variables (--toggle-dot / --toggle-dot-on / --toggle-dot-shadow) to control dot color and shadow for both states, ensuring clear visibility in both modes.
  • Review chart light-mode visibility fix — The review eval trend chart was too faint to see in light mode. Root cause: SVG stroke/fill attributes can't use CSS var(); the hardcoded #E8E8F0 (light line color) was nearly invisible on light background. Fixed: added 7 chart-specific CSS variables (--chart-line / --chart-fill / --chart-grid / --chart-axis / --chart-text-stroke / --chart-critical / --chart-critical-text). _buildEvalTrendSVG() reads these via getComputedStyle() and passes them to SVG attributes. Dark mode lines are light (#E8E8F0), light mode lines are dark (#4a4a52), ensuring the chart is clearly visible in both modes. Critical-move markers and labels also theme-aware.
  • Comprehensive sound supplement — Added playSound('select') to the global click event listener, providing unified audio feedback for ALL button clicks (quick toolbar, dialog buttons, setup buttons, color selection, SPID selection, time control selection, etc.). This complements the specialized sounds already in each function (e.g., undoMove's playSound('undo')); the audio engine's compressor prevents clipping overlap. All sounds are controlled by the 🔊/🔇 toggle.
🐛 Light Mode Not Switching with System Bug Fix (v1.0.8 Phase 22 fifth supplement)
  • Symptom — On Xiaomi HyperOS 3 with system global light mode enabled, the app still displayed in dark mode; the silver light-mode palette was not applied.
  • Root cause analysis (first principles) — Searched Android official docs (Darken web content in WebView) and found: WebView always sets prefers-color-scheme according to the app theme's isLightTheme attribute. The app uses Theme.NoTitleBar (not a DayNight theme), so isLightTheme does not change with the system dark mode toggle, causing WebView to pass a fixed prefers-color-scheme value. On some OEM ROMs (like Xiaomi HyperOS 3), this value may always be dark, so CSS @media(prefers-color-scheme:light) never matches.
  • Fix — Dual-channel theme detection for reliable switching on ALL devices:
    • Java layer: Added @JavascriptInterface isSystemDarkMode() method in StockfishNative.java that reads system night mode directly via UiModeManager.getNightMode() (compatible with Android 5.0 API 21+, including Xiaomi HyperOS 3). Supports MODE_NIGHT_NO (light), MODE_NIGHT_YES (dark), MODE_NIGHT_AUTO/MODE_NIGHT_CUSTOM (follows current system UI mode).
    • JS layer: _isLightMode() now prioritizes AndroidBridge.isSystemDarkMode(), falling back to window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: light)') (for desktop debugging).
    • CSS layer: Light theme variables in index.html.tpl and stats.html now trigger via BOTH @media(prefers-color-scheme:light) media query AND html[data-theme="light"] attribute selector. New _applySystemTheme() function sets document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light'/'dark') at startup based on AndroidBridge.isSystemDarkMode(), ensuring CSS variables switch correctly even if prefers-color-scheme is wrong.
  • Compatibility — This approach works reliably on all Android 5.0+ devices without depending on AppCompat.DayNight theme or AppCompatDelegate.setDefaultNightMode() (this app does not use the appcompat dependency). The dual-channel design (media query + attribute selector) ensures that even if one channel fails, the other still switches the theme correctly.
🔧 Comprehensive Code Review Optimization (v1.0.8 Phase 22 fourth supplement)
  • _isLightMode duplicate definition cleanup — _isLightMode() was defined identically in both ai-bridge.js and ui.js. Since build-chess.py merges modules in order (ai-bridge before ui), the ui.js definition silently overwrote the ai-bridge.js one — pure redundancy. Fixed: removed the ui.js duplicate; both files now use the ai-bridge.js definition.
  • _KING_PIECE_STYLE shared constant extraction — _loadingKingIconHTML() (ai-bridge.js) and _hdrKingIconHTML() (ui.js) had fully duplicated piece-styling code (color/stroke/glow/symbol). Extracted _KING_PIECE_STYLE shared constant (white/black objects); both functions now reference it. _loadingKingIconHTML uses typeof _KING_PIECE_STYLE!=='undefined' guard for load-order safety (ai-bridge loads before ui.js defines the constant).
  • .ver version badge theming — The .ver CSS class (version badge) still used hardcoded rgba(212,160,23,.15) background, showing gold tones in silver light mode. Fixed: replaced with var(--ev-bg) background and var(--border) border.
  • ANIMATION_DEFER_MS comment update — Comment previously only mentioned King 520ms, but Queen is now 500ms and also triggers heavy shake (450ms). Updated comment to clarify "King 520ms + Queen 500ms both trigger heavy shake; 560ms = 520+40 buffer".
  • 5 README.license files supplemented with v1.0.8 entries — src/main/assets/README.license, src/main/res/README.license, src/main/cpp/README.license, src/main/README.license, src/main/java/com/Regalia/README.license all lacked v1.0.8 changelog entries. Added: assets/ updated chess.html rebuild + stats.html silver; res/ + cpp/ unchanged; java/ updated 4 version constants.
🎨 Light Mode Silver Palette Redesign (v1.0.8 Phase 22 third supplement)
  • Elegant solemn silver tones — Light mode palette redesigned from warm cream (#f5ead6) to an elegant silver palette, inspired by polished silver chess sets:
    • Background: #f0f0f3 (silver-gray, soft and non-glare)
    • Card: #e0e0e5 (light silver-gray, subtle layering)
    • Text: #2c2c34 (deep slate, high-contrast readability)
    • Muted text: #6a6a76 (medium silver-gray)
    • Accent: #4a4a52 (deep silver-gray, buttons/links)
    • Border: #8a8a94 (silver-gray) / #5a5a66 (deep silver-gray primary)
    Forms a sharp contrast with dark mode's warm brown-red + bright gold — every color (except board squares & pieces) differs from dark mode, embodying the "day/night" visual transition.
  • Board & pieces unchanged — Board squares (SQ_LIGHT warm cream / SQ_DARK warm brown) and pieces (white #E8E8F0 silver-obsidian / black #1A1A2E deep-obsidian) remain identical in both modes, ensuring chess-readability is unaffected by theme switching.
  • 40+ hardcoded colors replaced with CSS variables — All component hardcoded colors in index.html.tpl (#ffd700, #1a0a0a, #221015, rgba(212,160,23,.15), etc.) replaced with CSS variables (var(--accent2), var(--bg), var(--card), var(--ev-bg), etc.). 15 new theme variables added (--btn-a-bg, --btn-g-bg, --btn-p-bg, --toggle-on-bg, --sq-hover, --scrollbar-track, --op-active-bg, --setup-del-hover, --setup-err-color, --mvar-color, --mnum-color, --last-to, --castle-ring, --setup-castle-mark, --setup-ep-mark).
  • New theme-aware utility classes — Added 4 utility classes (.hdr-btn / .hdr-btn-lg / .chip-active / .chip-inactive) in index.html.tpl to replace ui.js inline-style hardcoded colors, letting CSS variables cascade automatically in both themes.
  • ui.js + ai-bridge.js inline style theming — Replaced hardcoded colors in header buttons (ℹ️ / ↔️ language toggle), PGN cache chip buttons, recovery UI, ECO recommendation card, tablebase library card, review chart background, toggle dot, range slider. showToast() background/border/shadow also converted to CSS variables.
  • stats.html silver sync — Stats page light mode also updated to silver palette (#f0f0f3 bg / #2c2c34 text / #4a4a52 accent), maintaining visual consistency with the main app.
  • ♔/♚ king icon dark/light switch — Loading overlay and main header king icon auto-switch based on system theme: dark mode shows ♔ (white king, silver-obsidian #E8E8F0 + dark stroke + dark glow), light mode shows ♚ (black king, deep-obsidian #1A1A2E + light gold stroke + light gold glow), identical to on-board pieces. Follows Android (incl. Xiaomi HyperOS 3) system global dark mode toggle via prefers-color-scheme:light media query.
🔧 Sound & Animation Optimization (v1.0.8 Phase 22 second supplement)
  • Sound mute bug fix — Some sounds (piece-move sounds, castling sounds) were not controlled by the 🔊/🔇 sound toggle — they played even when muted. Root cause: _playPieceSound() / _playCastleSound() (in game-logic.js) called audioEngine.playXXX() directly, bypassing playSound()'s soundOn guard; also toggleSound() only toggled the soundOn global without syncing audioEngine.setEnabled(). Fix: (1) Added if(typeof soundOn!=='undefined'&&!soundOn)return; guard in _playPieceSound / _playCastleSound; (2) toggleSound() now calls audioEngine.setEnabled(soundOn), smoothly ramping the master gain to 0 via setTargetAtTime. After the fix, all sounds (including move sounds) are fully silenced when muted.
  • Queen animation optimization — heavier than rook, shake on par with king — As the strongest piece, the queen's original 420ms duration (only 130ms longer than rook's 290ms) with no landing shake felt insufficiently "heavy". Optimization: (1) Duration increased from 420ms to 500ms (close to king's 520ms, 210ms longer than rook's 290ms); (2) Easing changed from cubic-bezier(0.65,0,0.35,1) (elegant) to cubic-bezier(0.4,0,0.2,1) (same heavy easing as king); (3) Landing triggers _triggerBoardShake('heavy') (heavy shake 450ms, same as king — previously queen had no shake); (4) Scale variation increased from 0.05→0.08 for "heavy" feel; (5) Landing phase (t>0.9) adds compression landingScale for "impact". The queen's visual impact now matches the king, far heavier than the rook.
  • Move animation smoothness optimization — Reduced keyframe counts to lower GC pressure and improve smoothness: knight 24→18 keyframes, king 28→24, queen 20→16. Motion formulas and visual effects unchanged — only intermediate frame counts reduced. On 120Hz displays, each keyframe interval is ~15-25ms; fewer frames reduce Web Animations API internal interpolation computation and main-thread load.
  • Version number residue fix — Fixed 2 user-visible v1.0.7 residues: (1) game-logic.js's loading_title i18n string (loading overlay title) updated from "Regalia v1.0.7" to "Regalia v1.0.8"; (2) ChessWebViewClient.java's version comment updated from "Version: v1.0.7" to "Version: v1.0.8". Other "v1.0.7" references in code are historical Phase comments (e.g. // v1.0.7 PHASE 18) recording code change history — retained unchanged.
🔊 Scene Sound Expansion (v1.0.8 Phase 22 supplement)
  • First-principles analysis: "the essential purpose of sound is to provide auditory feedback, enhancing the user's perception of operation results and state changes." 14 new personified scene sounds were added, continuing the elegant-and-solemn sound style (pure Web Audio API synthesis + master→dry+reverb→compressor→destination routing chain):
    • Piece select (playSelect) — crisp short tone (sine 880→1320Hz rising), triggered when clicking own piece.
    • Deselect (playDeselect) — descending short tone (sine 880→560Hz), triggered when clicking the already-selected piece again; the reverse of the select sound.
    • Undo (playUndo) — reverse spin tone (triangle 660→330Hz descending), conveying "retraction".
    • Redo (playRedo) — forward spin tone (triangle 330→660Hz rising), conveying "redo"; symmetrical with undo.
    • Flip board (playFlip) — whoosh (sawtooth 200→800→200Hz + bandpass filter sweep 400→2000→400Hz), conveying "rotation".
    • New game (playNewGame) — fanfare three-note chord (triangle G-C-E 392/523/659Hz, 40ms spacing), solemn opening.
    • Enter review (playEnterReview) — contemplative tone (sine 220Hz + 330Hz overlay, long decay 0.5s), conveying "reflection".
    • Exit review (playExitReview) — return tone (sine 330→440Hz rising two-note), conveying "return to game".
    • Setup toggle (playSetupToggle) — wood-place tone (triangle 180→120Hz short), conveying "placing pieces".
    • Resign (playResign) — flag-lower tone (sine A-F-C 440/349/262Hz descending three-note, increasing decay), solemn and mournful.
    • Copy success (playCopy) — crisp ding (sine 1200→1800Hz short rising), triggered on successful FEN/PGN copy.
    • Operation error (playError) — low error tone (square 220→110Hz descending + bandpass noise burst), triggered on operation failure.
    • AI think start (playAiThinkStart) — soft tick (sine 1000Hz, 50ms), triggered when engine starts searching.
    • AI think end (playAiThinkEnd) — soft acknowledgement (sine 600+800Hz two-note), triggered when engine returns bestmove, conveying "got it".
  • Smart toast sound — showToast() adds _playToastSound(msg) helper that auto-detects sound type from message content: detects "已复制/已导出/已保存/成功/copied/exported/saved" keywords to play playCopy; detects "失败/错误/超时/不可用/拒绝/无法/不能/failed/error/timeout/unavailable/rejected" keywords to play playError; neutral messages play no sound (avoiding sound fatigue). This avoids modifying all 76 showToast call sites — sound is intelligently inferred from message content.
  • Sound toggle feedback — toggleSound() plays playSelect immediately when turning sound ON, giving the user audible confirmation; plays nothing when turning OFF (silent by definition).
  • Language toggle feedback — toggleLang() plays playSelect on Chinese/English switch, providing operation confirmation.
  • AI hint feedback — getHint() plays playHint (soft triangle wave 660Hz) when requesting AI hint; previously this method was defined but never called.
  • playSound signature unchanged — playSound(type) signature preserved; type parameter expanded from 7 to 21 values (14 new scene sounds added). All new sounds are triggered via the audioEngine global instance, sharing the same routing chain and reverb with existing piece sounds.
🐛 Bug Fixes (post-release emergency fixes for v1.0.8 Phase 22)
  • _landingAnimActive undefined error after move — v1.0.8 initial release removed the _landingAnimActive variable (landing animation replaced by Web Animations API overlay), but 3 residual references were missed:
    (1) ai-bridge.js engine-error handler's _landingAnimActive=false; and _landingAnimTimer cleanup — removed (animation state now managed solely by animationInProgress).
    (2) game-logic.js _requestStockfishMove()'s if(!_landingAnimActive)render(); — changed to if(!animationInProgress)render(); (the new overlay is an independent layer that doesn't block render; full render is only skipped while a piece-move animation is active).
    (3) ui.js _updateSingleSq()'s sig signature variable's trailing +animCls — removed (the animCls variable was deleted in the prior cleanup; the residual reference caused ReferenceError).
    Root cause: The v1.0.8 redesign used MultiEdit to batch-replace main reference points, but these 3 spots in different code paths (engine-error handler, AI request, lightweight update signature) were not covered. After the fix, moves no longer throw errors.
  • Extra semicolon next to king icon ♔/♚ — The _hdrKingIconHTML() function used ♚\uFE0E; and ♔\uFE0E;, where \uFE0E is a Unicode escape (Variation Selector-15, text-presentation selector) and the trailing semicolon ; was a literal character being displayed. Fixed to \u265A\uFE0E (black king) and \u2654\uFE0E (white king), removing the extra semicolon. Also unified _loadingKingIconHTML() to use Unicode escapes instead of literal ♚/♔ characters for encoding safety.
  • Duplicate move sound playback — executeMove()'s playSound('move'/'capture'/'castle') duplicated the sound triggered by animateMove()'s internal _playPieceSound() / _playCastleSound(). Fixed: executeMove() now only handles special cases that animateMove doesn't cover — playSound('promote') (promotion arpeggio) and playSound('check') (check alert tone, overlaid on top of the piece sound). Plain move and capture sounds are triggered entirely by animateMove based on piece type, avoiding double-sound. Haptic feedback (HapticManager) logic unchanged.
  • Animation timing / deferred-callback mismatch — ANIMATION_DEFER_MS was 300ms (matching the old 240-340ms CSS transitions), but the new personified animations last up to 520ms (King). On a king move, the 300ms deferred callback would fire updateAfterMove() → render() before the animation finished; while the animationInProgress guard throttled the render, this wasted a throttle cycle. Fixed: ANIMATION_DEFER_MS increased to 560ms (King 520ms + 40ms buffer) so the deferred callback fires only after the animation completes.
  • Stale animation closure DOM leakage — In _finishAnim(), when _myGen!==_animGen (stale closure, newer animation started), the function returned early without removing the overlay nodes (el/rookEl) it had created, causing DOM leakage. Fixed: moved el.remove() / rookEl.remove() before the _myGen check, ensuring overlay nodes are always cleaned up (even if the closure is stale). Global state writes remain guarded by _myGen.
  • Redundant CSS variable cleanup — The :root defined 4 CSS variables (--hdr-king-color / --hdr-king-stroke / --hdr-king-shadow / --hdr-king-sym) that were never referenced (king icon switching is implemented by the JS function _hdrKingIconHTML()). Removed the redundant definitions.

Version: Upgraded to versionCode=108, versionName="1.0.8". Engine: Stockfish 18 arm64-v8a-dotprod (unchanged). APK signature: v1+v2+v3 triple signing complete, compatible with Xiaomi HyperOS 3. Source tar: All engine files excluded. Build environment: JDK 21 (Temurin 21.0.5), Android SDK 35, NDK 27.2.12479018, CMake 3.22.1, build-tools 34.0.0.

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 21 New (Bug Fixes: portrait dialog positioning precision fix, landscape anti-shake clipping root-cause fix, move-history panel clipping fix, 2026.6.30)

This phase fixes 2 adjustments from Phase 20 that did not achieve the intended effect, plus an additional fix for the landscape move-history panel being partially hidden.

🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 21)
  • Portrait dialog positioning precision fix (slightly above center) — Phase 20 used padding-top:18vh;padding-bottom:10px to position dialogs "slightly above center", but the actual computed result placed the dialog center at ~59vh (slightly BELOW center), the opposite of the intent. Root cause: align-items:center centers the dialog within the content area (after padding). Content area center = 18vh + (100vh - 18vh - 10px)/2 ≈ 59vh. Fix: Changed to padding-top:10px;padding-bottom:12vh. Content area center = 10px + (100vh - 10px - 12vh)/2 ≈ 44vh, precisely achieving "slightly above center". The fullscreen dialog (New Game Settings) uses negative margins to cancel both paddings, maintaining true full-screen fill.
  • Landscape anti-shake clipping root-cause fix + rollback of ineffective margin — Phase 20 added margin-right:10px to .bsec to prevent anti-shake translation from being clipped, but the user reported it was still clipped. Root cause: The clipping happens at .bsec's own overflow:hidden boundary, NOT at the gap between .bsec and .panel — margin-right only increases the gap and does not affect internal clipping. Deeper root cause: _recalcCellSize() had _antiShake=isLandscape?0:6 (landscape reserved 0), so the board width calculation did not reserve space for the ±8px anti-shake translation. Fix: (1) Rolled back the .bsec margin-right:10px (restored to original); (2) Changed .bsec to overflow-x:visible;overflow-y:hidden so the .bwrap.stabilized translate3d is not clipped; (3) _antiShake now reserves 8px in BOTH orientations (matching StabilizationHelper.MAX_DISPLACEMENT_PX=8.0f), ensuring the CELL calculation leaves space for the anti-shake translation.
  • Landscape move-history panel clipping fix — In landscape mode, the move-history panel (.mlist inside .panel) had wide content clipped by .main{overflow-x:hidden}, preventing the user from scrolling to see it. Root cause: .panel only had overflow-y:auto with no overflow-x setting, so wide content overflowed into .main and was clipped. Fix: Added overflow-x:auto to .panel so wide content scrolls WITHIN the panel instead of being clipped at the page level.

Version: versionCode=107, versionName="1.0.7" unchanged. Engine: Stockfish 18 arm64-v8a-dotprod (unchanged). APK Signature: v1+v2+v3 triple signing, compatible with Xiaomi HyperOS 3. Source tar: All engine files excluded.

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 20 New (UX Refinements: enlarged review eval bar / analyze button, slowed move animation, landscape anti-shake clipping fix, portrait dialog positioning, 2026.6.30)

This phase refines 4 UX details based on user feedback, improving visual comfort and operation fluency.

🎨 UX Optimizations (v1.0.7 Phase 20)
  • Review "Eval Bar" and "Analyze All" button enlarged — Eval bar font increased from .75rem/.7rem (portrait/landscape) to .85rem/.8rem; emoji from .95rem to 1.1rem/1.05rem; max-height relaxed from 1.9em to 2.4em; padding increased from 3px 8px to 5px 10px. "Analyze All" button font increased from .7rem to .8rem; min-height from 28px to 34px; padding from default to 6px 10px. Text and emoji now display fully with comfortable breathing room — no longer cramped. Other buttons in the landscape .review-bottom area are also slightly enlarged (.55rem→.65rem, 22px→26px) for visual harmony.
  • Move animation slowed ~30% — Per-piece move animation durations adjusted from 180-260ms to 240-340ms (pawn 180→240, knight 240→320, bishop 210→280, rook 180→240, queen 260→340, king 210→280), so the human eye can clearly follow the smooth motion. CSS transition durations updated to match the JS durations table. 120fps high-frame-rate is preserved — the animation is GPU-composited via will-change:transform + translate3d, and the browser renders at the display's native refresh rate; the cubic-bezier(.25,.1,.25,1) easing curve is unchanged — only the duration is longer.
  • Landscape board right-side clearance increased — In landscape mode, .bsec (board section) now has margin-right:10px, providing ample buffer for the anti-shake translation (.bwrap.stabilized applies ±8px translate3d). Previously, when anti-shake was enabled, the board's right edge could be clipped by .main's overflow-x:hidden when shifted rightward. The 10px clearance covers the 8px max displacement + 2px breathing room, ensuring the board remains fully visible throughout the anti-shake range.
  • Portrait dialog positioning optimized — In portrait mode, all dialogs (resign confirm, about, import, save-PGN prompt, PGN cache manager) are repositioned from "geometric dead-center" to "slightly above screen center". Previously .dov used align-items:center with equal top/bottom padding, which on tall phones with status bars / notches made dialogs feel too high (cramped against the top). Now uses asymmetric padding (padding-top:18vh;padding-bottom:10px) so the effective center moves down to ~40% screen height — visually "slightly above center" and more comfortable. The fullscreen dialog (New Game Settings) uses negative margin to cancel the padding-top, maintaining true full-screen fill.
