🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 19 New (Comprehensive First-Principles Code Review: 7 subagents reviewed 28k lines in parallel, 20+ critical fixes implemented, 2026.6.30)

This phase performed a line-by-line first-principles code review of all 20 source files (28,281 lines). 7 subagents reviewed different file groups in parallel (game-logic + chess960, ai-bridge, ui in 3 segments, PGN parsing 3 files, HTML/CSS 2 files, Java 9 files + JNI). 20+ optimizations implemented by priority: bug fix > functionality > performance > redundancy cleanup > simplification.

🐛 Critical Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 19)
  • _reviewEvalCache Corruption Race (Critical) — requestEngineEval's cache-hit and terminal-position (checkmate/draw) fast paths did not clear the pending debounce timer. A stale debounce timer capturing a PRIOR step's FEN could fire after the cache-hit return, pass the staleness filter (reviewStep matches), and overwrite the current step's correct cached eval — permanently corrupting the cache. Fix: Clear _reviewEvalDebounceTimer and increment _evalStaleGen on both fast paths to invalidate any in-flight callback.
  • Cross-Mode Stale Callback Race (Critical) — onEngineEval's two filters are mode-exclusive: review mode checks _reviewEvalRequestedStep !== reviewStep, normal mode checks _evalStaleGen !== _evalRequestGen. After exiting review, a review-mode callback still in flight would pass the normal-mode gen check (both gens equal) and overwrite the correct eval for up to 30s. Fix: Capture mode at request time (_evalRequestReviewMode); reject cross-mode callbacks in onEngineEval.
  • animateMove Reduced-Motion Path Race — Phase 18 added _animGen generation counter and _animFinishTimer cancellation, but the reduced-motion early-return path was not updated. A prior non-reduced-motion animation's stale _finishAnim closure could fire and overwrite _lastAnimTarget with the OLD target. Fix: Reduced-motion path now cancels _animFinishTimer, increments _animGen, and sets the 3 missing flags.
  • reviewAnalyzeAll Completion Doesn't Restore Eval Vars + reviewCritical Not Recomputed — _reviewAnalyzeAdvance's completion branch manually set reviewStep/gameState but never restored _sfEval etc. from cache — the eval bar showed the LAST analyzed step's eval instead of the returned step's eval. Also reviewCritical was never recomputed — 💥/❌ markers stayed missing after Analyze All on a fresh game. Fix: Call reviewGoTo(returnStep) (which restores from cache) and call _findCriticalMoves() to recompute critical moves.
  • PGN [%eval] Placeholder Offset (Critical) — When a PGN starts with a [FEN] where Black is to move, importPGN prepends a null placeholder at moveRecords[0], but _parsePGN's reviewStep computation doesn't know about this placeholder — evals attach to the wrong step, invisible on PGN re-export, and misaligned in review mode. Fix: Apply _placeholderOffset when populating the eval/annotation/comment caches.
  • setupRedoStack Not Cleared — Setup mode's "Reset Board" and "Clear Board" buttons cleared setupHistory but not setupRedoStack. The redo button stayed clickable and applied stale entries to the empty board. Fix: Added setupRedoStack=[] to both onclick handlers.
  • _resignGame Clock Leak — gameClocks.running=false was a no-op (the field doesn't exist); the 200ms interval kept firing for the rest of the session, wasting CPU. Fix: Use clearInterval(gameClockTimerId) instead.
  • _pendingStatsImportPGN Global Race — The stats-page import-back PGN was passed via a module-level global stash. If the function was called twice before the first save-prompt resolved, the second call overwrote the stash and the first import was silently lost. Fix: Close over pgnText directly; removed the global stash.
  • stats.html Backspace Re-opens Dismissed Dialog — The global keydown handler unconditionally called returnToGame(), which re-showed the import-back prompt whenever _statsImportedPGN was set. After dismissing with Cancel, the next Backspace immediately re-opened it — trapping keyboard users. Fix: Check _statsImportBackDialogVisible flag; if visible, call _statsImportBackDismiss().
  • stats.html Double safe-area-inset-top — Both body and .hdr applied env(safe-area-inset-top). Before scrolling the title sat at 2×safe-top + 8px; when sticky locked it jumped to safe-top — a visible "header snaps upward" glitch on first scroll. Fix: body top padding is now 0; .hdr owns the top safe-area via padding-top:calc(10px + env(safe-area-inset-top)).
  • StockfishNative Thread Safety: volatile Fields — engineProcess/engineReader/engineWriter/readerThread/_engineExecutor were written from multiple threads without volatile/synchronization — a read on one thread may never observe a null write from another, producing NPEs or writes to a destroyed process's stream. Fix: All declared volatile.
  • stopAndWaitForBestmove Timeout Stale Bestmove Corruption — When the engine didn't respond to "stop" within 1 second, _stopLatch was nulled in finally, and the eventual late bestmove fell through to handleBestMove as a real move — potentially generating an AI move for the wrong position, corrupting game state. Fix: On timeout, set _discardingPonderBestmove = true to discard the late bestmove.
  • ChessApp UncaughtExceptionHandler Swallows Error — Worker-thread Errors (OOM/StackOverflow/NoClassDefFoundError) were silently swallowed, leaving the JVM in a corrupted state — e.g. if SF-Reader died from OOM, the engine silently stopped responding while isProcessAlive() still returned true, causing a 30-120s apparent hang. Fix: Error subclasses are now chained to the default handler so the process dies cleanly and restarts.
  • EngineService.lastStatusInfo Not volatile — Written from the JS binder thread, read from the service main thread — stale reads caused the notification to display an old status. Fix: Declared volatile.
  • probeTablebase JSON Parse Error Miscounts as Offline — A resp.json() parse failure threw into the generic catch, incrementing _tbFailCount — 3 such responses would set _tbOffline for 60 seconds, contradicting the Rev62 fix that excluded 4xx errors for the same reason (server is reachable). Fix: JSON parsing now has its own try/catch returning null without incrementing the fail count.
🔧 Performance & Functionality (v1.0.7 Phase 19)
  • Notification Throttle Drops Last Pending Info — When the engine stopped emitting progress during the 1s throttle window, the last-seen info was silently dropped. Fix: Added _pendingNotificationInfo buffer; the throttle timer flushes it on expiry.
  • PGN Export Eval Tag Uses peek() Instead of get() — _buildPGNString's _reviewEvalCache.get(i+1) refreshed LRU order, pushing the current game's evals to the newest end and evicting OTHER games' evals. Fix: Changed to peek() (read-only, no side effect).
  • WDL Negative Percentage — lp=100-wp-dp could be -1 at rounding boundaries (e.g. W=99.5,D=0.5,L=0 → wp=100,dp=1,lp=-1). Fix: Compute lp=Math.round(L/total*100) directly; the three may sum to 99 or 101.
  • onEngineError Restart Timer Leak — The 1500ms restart timer was untracked; if the engine auto-recovered before it fired, it would spuriously restart an already-ready engine. Fix: Track _engineErrorRestartTimer; cancel in onEngineReady.
  • stats.html CSP Added — The stats page renders user-pasted PGN content but had no Content Security Policy — no defense-in-depth for XSS bypasses. Fix: Added a CSP matching chess.html (default-src 'none'; script-src 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'unsafe-inline'; img-src data:; connect-src 'none').
🧹 Redundancy Cleanup (v1.0.7 Phase 19)
  • Removed stale "Unlimited cache size" comment in ai-bridge.js (Phase 18 already added MAX_ENTRIES=2000).
  • Removed dead code renderPGN() and renderMoveNotation() from stats.html (superseded by renderPGNText() in v1.0.3 but never deleted; renderMoveNotation was a no-op stub).
  • Removed duplicate body rule in stats.html portrait media query (byte-identical to the base rule).

Source tar: All engine files excluded. Review method: 7 subagents reviewed 28k lines in parallel, line-by-line first-principles analysis.

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 18 New (_reviewEvalCache LRU Eviction + Review Move List Virtual List + 11 First-Principles Code Review Fixes, 2026.6.30)

This phase completes the two remaining architectural suggestions from the Kimi audit report (LRU cache eviction + virtual list), and performs a first-principles line-by-line code review of all source files, implementing 11 optimizations by priority: bug fix > functionality > performance > redundancy cleanup > simplification.

⚡ Performance Breakthroughs (v1.0.7 Phase 18)
  • _reviewEvalCache LRU Eviction — The old _reviewEvalCache comment claimed "Unlimited cache size", arguing 60k entries ≈ 12MB was "negligible". First-principles analysis found three errors: (1) JSON persistence size was underestimated (~400B/entry not ~200B, 60k entries ≈ 24MB JSON); (2) synchronous JSON.stringify blocks the main thread 100-300ms (perceptible on mid-tier phones); (3) WebView localStorage actual quota is ~5MB, 24MB throws QuotaExceededError which was silently caught → backup path silently failed. Fix: Added MAX_ENTRIES=2000 soft cap (~800KB JSON, well under any quota), _evictIfOverCap() triggers on set(), evicting oldest entries by Map insertion order (= LRU order, get/set refresh order via delete+set). Key design: Does NOT evict _reviewEvalRequestedStep (the step the user is currently viewing) to avoid "analyzing..." flicker; TDZ-safe (_reviewEvalRequestedStep is initialized by the time the closure runs); persistence preserves LRU order (Array.from(m.entries())); backward-compatible (persisted files >2000 entries are auto-evicted on first set()). Normal single-game use (~80 steps) never triggers eviction.
  • Review Move List Virtual List — The old review move list rebuilt ~400 DOM nodes for 200+ move games via app.innerHTML = h on every render(). Fix: When move count > 80 (RV_VIRTUAL_THRESHOLD), enable virtual list — render only viewport + 10 rows overscan (RV_OVERSCAN) as DOM nodes, with top/bottom spacer <div>s for total scroll height. Key design: Extracted shared _buildReviewMovesInnerHTML(start, end) eliminating ~40 lines of landscape/portrait duplication; passive scroll listener (passive:true, cannot block scrolling or interfere with scroll-restore); 80ms-debounced _refreshReviewMovesOnly() replaces only .review-moves innerHTML (preserves board/eval bar/chart/nav/dialog state); first render measures avg row height via requestAnimationFrame (initial estimate 44px, measured to accommodate variation 🌿 expanded 2-3x row height); _forceReviewWindowToStep() ensures reviewGoTo() target is in window; _resetRvVirtualState() resets on enter/exit review, new game, PGN/FEN import. Performance: Not enabled under 80 steps (full render faster for short lists); long-game render cost reduced from O(total moves) to O(visible + overscan).
🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 18)
  • Chess960 Castling unmakeMv Board Corruption (Critical) — Symptom: In ~half of Chess960 SP-ID positions (e.g. white king starts on f1, kingside castle), makeMvInPlace → unmakeMv round-trip corrupts the board: king appears at rook's source, rook vanishes. Root cause: unmakeMv step 2 restores the king at f (king source), but the rook's destination cr.to may equal f (rook moved to king's old square) — step 2 already overwrote the rook with the king; step 4 s.board[cr.from] = s.board[cr.to] reads the king (not the rook), copies the king to the rook's source, and nulls cr.to — king ends up at rook's source, rook lost. Fix: makeMvInPlace saves the rook piece itself in undo.castlingRook.piece, not relying on board state; unmakeMv restores the rook from the saved piece, and only nulls cr.to if it does not coincide with king source f. This bug affected search state, checkmate/stalemate detection, and SAN disambiguation, but was masked by single-ply search — deeper JS search would expose it immediately.
  • makeMvInPlace Fails to Clear Castling Rights for Rook Move/Capture — makeMvInPlace steps 6/7 called findCastlingRooks(s.board) after the rook had already moved (step 3) or been captured (step 1), so findCastlingRooks could not find the rook at its source — castling right was NOT cleared. Fix: Snapshot the castling-rights delta before mutating the board (_movingRookSide / _capturedRookSide); steps 6/7 use the snapshot instead of re-calling findCastlingRooks. Also removes two redundant scans per rook move/capture (small perf win).
  • animateMove Stale-_finishAnim Race Condition — When a new animation started within dur+60ms of the previous one, the old setTimeout(_finishAnim) was NOT cancelled — the stale closure would fire and corrupt the new animation's global state (animationInProgress=false, _lastAnimTarget=oldTarget, _activeAnimEls=[] orphaning the new overlay). Fix: Module-level _animFinishTimer + _animGen generation counter; on entry, cancel the pending timer and bump the generation; _finishAnim self-invalidates if its generation is stale.
  • Single-Step Review Eval Missing Safety Timer — The old code had a 30s safety timer for normal game mode and a 60s/step timer for batch analyze-all, but NO safety net for single-step review eval — if the engine hung, the eval bar stayed stuck at "analyzing..." forever. Fix: Added a 45s safety timer in the debounced review eval path (depth-22 evals need 20-25s, leaving a 20s margin), cleared by onEngineEval on success.
  • Virtual List Window Forced Back to Active Step on Every Render — The old code forced the window to contain the active step on every render(), even when the user had scrolled away and reviewStep hadn't changed — discarding the user's scroll position and causing a triple-flicker (active-step rows → blank spacer → user-scrolled rows). Fix: Track _lastRenderReviewStep; only force the window when reviewStep changed or on first virtual render; the user's scroll position is now preserved across renders that don't change reviewStep.
  • _rvScrollRefreshTimer Not Cleared in renderInternal — A pending 80ms debounce timer could fire AFTER app.innerHTML=h and rebuild .review-moves with a stale window conflicting with the window render() just computed — visible flicker. Fix: Clear _rvScrollRefreshTimer in renderInternal after the innerHTML assignment.
  • PGN/FEN Import Paths Missing _resetRvVirtualState — _doPastePGN / _importFENWithSaveCheck / _importPGNFileWithSaveCheck did not reset virtual list state, so stale avgRowH/measured from a previous long game could carry over. Fix: Added _resetRvVirtualState() calls at the start of each import wrapper (defense in depth — enterReview() already resets, but this covers the gap between import and the next review session).
  • pgn-standard.js Comment Flattening Pollutes Movetext (Latent) — parseStandardPGN's comment-flattening loop stripped only the braces and left the comment body as bare text — the tokenizer then classified each whitespace-delimited comment word as a spurious SAN token, polluting the move list. Fix: Match the proven-correct pattern in tablebase.js:456 — remove entire comments (braces + body); added unclosed-brace truncation matching tablebase.js:460-464. (Latent: function currently unused, but prevents a landmine if ever wired in.)
  • worker-pool.js Missing Unclosed-Brace Handling (Latent) — The worker PGN parser's brace-flattening loop did not handle unclosed braces; an unclosed { survived and polluted the token stream, inconsistent with the main-thread parser. Fix: Added truncation at first unclosed brace.
🔧 Performance & Redundancy Cleanup (v1.0.7 Phase 18)
  • Removed Redundant innerHTML Write in reviewGoTo — reviewGoTo() called _forceReviewWindowToStep() which did an innerHTML replacement immediately overwritten by the subsequent render()'s app.innerHTML=h — pure waste. Fix: Removed the redundant call; render()'s window-computation block already handles the step change correctly.
  • Removed Dead Code in animateMove — The if(isCheck){const ck=pieceColor==='white'?null:null} block had ck always null and never read; the comment was also misleading. Removed the dead block.

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 17 Additions (Chess960 "king self-capture" critical bug fix + review "Analyze All" button auto-refresh + adoption of reasonable Kimi-audit suggestions, 2026.6.29)

This phase fixes 2 critical bugs left over from Phase 16, and adopts 5 reasonable suggestions from the Kimi audit report (rejecting suggestions that would require major architectural changes for uncertain benefit — incremental DOM rendering, virtual scrolling, LRU eval cache, Worker source modularization, AST parsing — keeping only small, low-risk improvements consistent with the existing code style).

🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 17)
  • Chess960 castling "king self-capture" critical bug — Symptom: In Chess960 mode, when the king's starting position happens to be on its castling destination square (e.g. an SP-ID where white king starts on g1), performing kingside castling causes the king to "capture itself" and vanish from the board. Root cause: The castling branch of makeMv() / makeMvInPlace() unconditionally executes ns.board[to.row][to.col] = ns.board[from.row][from.col]; ns.board[from.row][from.col] = null;. When from === to (king already on its target), the second line NULLS the king's own square — the king vanishes. Associated issues: unmakeMv() would similarly null the king's square; animateMove() would create a dx=0, dy=0 "no-op" animation overlay. Fix: When castling AND from === to, skip the king's move entirely (makeMv/makeMvInPlace only move the rook from source to destination, king stays put); unmakeMv detects castlingRook presence + from===to and skips the king-position restore (the rook is independently restored via the castlingRook field); animateMove in this case skips the king animation overlay and only animates the rook. This fix matches the Fischer Random Chess rule: "Castling in place — if the king or rook's initial position happens to be its castling destination, castling is still legal as long as all conditions are met; that piece 'stays put' while the other piece moves to its designated position." A 20-case Node-sandbox regression test is added at /home/z/my-project/scripts/test-chess960-castling.js, covering: king on g1 kingside castle, king on c1 queenside castle, king on f1 + rook on g1 swap-position castle, makeMvInPlace+unmakeMv round-trip fidelity, and standard castling non-regression.
  • Review "Analyze All" button state not auto-updating — Symptom: After the user manually evaluates every step by clicking through the move list one by one, the "Analyze All" button does not automatically switch to "All Analyzed" state. Root cause: onEngineEval() on manual-eval completion only calls _updateAllEvalDisplays() (which refreshes the eval bar / move list), never the analyze button. The button label is recomputed ONLY inside the full renderInternal() pass; after the user manually evaluates the LAST step by clicking its row, no event triggers a render, so the button never refreshes. Fix: Extract the button-label computation into a pure function _rvAnalyzeBtnLabel(); give the button id="review-analyze-btn"; add _updateReviewAnalyzeBtn() that refreshes the label directly via textContent (one getElementById + one textContent write — extremely cheap, no DOM rebuild, no scroll-position interference); call _updateReviewAnalyzeBtn() at the end of onEngineEval(). Whether via batch "Analyze All" or manual step-by-step evaluation, the button now switches to "All Analyzed" the moment the last step's eval completes.
🎨 Adopted Reasonable Kimi-Audit Suggestions (v1.0.7 Phase 17)

The Kimi audit report proposed 30+ suggestions. After case-by-case screening, the following 5 are adopted (consistent with existing code style, low risk, clear benefit). The remaining suggestions (incremental DOM rendering, virtual scrolling, LRU for _reviewEvalCache, Worker source modularization, AST parsing, etc.) would require major architectural changes or offer uncertain benefit, and are not implemented in this phase.

  • stats.html _escFEN backtick escaping — _escFEN() previously escaped & < > " ' (5 chars) but not the backtick. Added ` → &#96;, closing a residual template-literal injection vector. Backticks in PGN comments are rare but legal; escaping them has no side effects.
  • stats.html selectVariationMove uses hand-written _cloneStatsState instead of JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(state)) deep clone — The parsed.moves[].state object has a known, stable shape (board 8×8 array, currentTurn, castlingRights, enPassantTarget, halfMoveClock, fullMoveNumber, wk, bk) — no Map/Set/undefined/circular refs. The hand-rolled _cloneStatsState() is ~10x faster than JSON serialize/parse, and is type-safe (JSON silently drops future fields; hand-rolled clone forces explicit declaration).
  • chess.html main board .bgrid gets content-visibility:auto — When the board is scrolled off-screen (e.g. long stats panels, future split-view layouts), the browser can skip its rendering work. contain:strict is NOT added (it would freeze the grid's intrinsic size and break the JS responsive CELL recalculation); .sq already has contain:layout style paint, so child-paint cost is already optimized.
  • chess.html animateMove() honors prefers-reduced-motion on the JS side too — The CSS @media(prefers-reduced-motion:reduce) already disables CSS animations, but the JS path still creates overlay <div>s, attaches transitionend listeners, and triggers double-rAF — wasted work that also leaves the board in a transient state for one frame (source piece hidden). Added a window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)') check; when matched, the entire animation path is skipped, matching the user's OS-level accessibility preference (Android "Remove animations" / iOS "Reduce Motion" / desktop browser setting).
  • stats.html board max-width raised from 360px to 400px — Kimi suggested removing the cap entirely or switching to container queries. After weighing, the adopted change is a "modest relaxation": the board gets a bit more breathing room on tablets / wide landscape phones, without dominating the stats panel on tablets (the panel itself is already width-capped, and an unbounded board would crowd out the surrounding statistics). No impact on phones (the parent panel is already width-capped).

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 16 Additions (final comprehensive review: PGN [%eval] import off-by-one fix + multiple redundancy cleanups, 2026.6.29)

This phase performs a final line-by-line first-principles review of all source files, fixing one PGN-import logic bug and cleaning up multiple redundant code blocks and comments.

🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 16)
  • PGN import [%eval] comment attaches to wrong reviewStep (off-by-one) — Root cause: in tablebase.js's _parsePGN, [%eval] comments are attached to _extractedEvals either "when the next move is seen" or "at end-of-loop". But per PGN/Lichess convention, [%eval] describes the position AFTER the move in whose comment it appears. In 1. e4 {[%eval 0.2]} e5, the [%eval 0.2] describes the post-e4 position (reviewStep=1), but by the time e5 is seen _moveCount has incremented to 2 and the code attaches to reviewStep=2 (post-e5) — wrong. Worse, the trailing case 1. e4 {[%eval 0.2]} (no following move) attaches to _moveCount+1=2, which is beyond reviewStates.length (=2; valid reviewSteps are 0..1) — that eval is never read. This bug also defeated Phase 15's "step 0 cacheable" goal for PGN imports: a leading {[%eval 0.5]} 1. e4 should attach to reviewStep=0 (initial position) but attached to reviewStep=1. Fix: mid-branch changed to reviewStep:_moveCount-1 (the previous move's post-position); trailing branch changed to reviewStep:_moveCount (the last move's post-position). The leading case now correctly attaches to reviewStep=0.
🧹 Redundancy Cleanup (v1.0.7 Phase 16)
  • Removed worker-pool.js second rawTokens walk — In worker-pool.js's PGN parser, the first loop already collects all non-variation tokens into rootFrame.tokens (variation-internal tokens go to their own frames via the stack push/pop triggered by (/)). The second loop re-walked rawTokens to rebuild the same mainTokens list — redundant. Now reuses rootFrame.tokens directly.
  • Removed redundant selective cache-clear in importPGN — tablebase.js's importPGN already calls _reviewEvalCache.clear() (full clear) at the top, but the later [%eval]-populate block had a loop deleting entries 0..moveRecords.length+1 "to preserve other games' entries" — the full clear already removed everything, so the loop was dead code and its comment was stale. Removed the redundant loop and stale comment.
  • Removed unused varStack variable in pgn-standard.js — let varStack=null; was declared but never read or assigned; deleted.
  • Removed dead ternary in _findCriticalMoves — (moverDelta>0?'+':'') in the moverDelta>300 branch: moverDelta>0 is always true at that point (entry condition is moverDelta>300), so the ternary is dead. Simplified to a literal ' +'.
  • Updated stale "1-based" comments — Phase 15 changed _reviewEvalCache's keying to 0-based (step 0 = initial position), but 4 comments in ai-bridge.js and ui.js still said "keyed by reviewStep (1-based)". Synchronized to "0-based since v1.0.7 Phase 15".
  • Removed 3 debug console.logs — The three "populated N eval/visual-annotation/free-text entries from PGN comments" debug logs in importPGN are logcat noise in production; removed. Also removed the _populated/_populatedVa/_populatedCm counters that existed solely to feed those logs (declared, incremented, never read).

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 15 Additions (review "Analyze All" now includes step 0 — the initial position, 2026.6.29)

This phase extends the review screen's "Analyze All" feature to include step 0 (the initial position). Previously "Analyze All" only analyzed steps 1..N (positions after each move), skipping step 0 — which meant the first move's delta/classification could not be displayed (because _prevMvEval=peek(0) returned null), and the trend chart lacked a real data point at x=0.

🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 15)
  • "Analyze All" skipped step 0 (the initial position) — Root cause: reviewAnalyzeAll() and _reviewAnalyzeAdvance() previously iterated starting from step 1, and the UI's _totalSteps=moveRecords.length did not count step 0. This caused: (1) the initial position's eval was never computed; (2) the first move in the move list had no delta/classification label (because peek(0) returned null, failing the _mvEval!=null&&_prevMvEval!=null check); (3) the trend chart lacked a real data point at x=0; (4) _findCriticalMoves()'s critical-move detection for the first move was ineffective. Fix: _totalSteps is now moveRecords.length+1 (includes step 0); reviewAnalyzeAll()'s all-cached check and start-step search now use for(let i=0;i<=_lastStep;i++); _reviewAnalyzeAdvance()'s completion toast and progress toast now use _lastStep+1 (includes step 0). "Analyze All" now starts from step 0 — the initial position's eval is cached, and the first move's delta/classification, the chart's starting point, and critical-move detection all work.
🎨 Feature Polish (v1.0.7 Phase 15)
  • Zero-move positions can now be analyzed — When moveRecords.length===0 (only the initial position, no moves), _totalSteps=1, the "Analyze All" button shows "Analyze All 1", and clicking it analyzes step 0. Previously _totalSteps=0 and _allCached was always false due to the _totalSteps>0 guard, so the button showed "Analyze All 0" and analysis could not be triggered.

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 13 Additions (misreport cleanup + first-principles code review, 2026.6.29)

This phase confirms that the 'review-mode ⚡ marker position anomaly' fixed in Phases 9-11 was a misreport — the root cause never existed, and the associated defensive code and comments became redundant. This phase precisely removes the redundancy with no residue, and fixes one real bug discovered during the cleanup.

🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 13)
  • enterReview() replay-loop no-piece branch shared reference — In enterReview(), the !piece branch (move record points to an empty square — should not happen but has a defensive log) did reviewStates.push({state:s,...}) referencing s directly without cloneS(s). Since this branch does not reassign s, the entry would share the same s reference with the next iteration's state (in practice harmless because makeMv returns a fresh object and reassigns s, but inconsistent with the other two push sites). Fix: unified to cloneS(s), matching the null-placeholder and success branches.
🧹 Redundancy Cleanup (v1.0.7 Phase 13)
  • Removed the setupMode defensive guard in computeVisibleEpMark() — The && typeof setupMode!=='undefined' && setupMode clause in if(s.setupEpMark && ...) was a defense added for the misreport. First-principles analysis: setupEpMark is a setup-only transient field — toggleSetup() sets it on entry and clears it on exit, and initState()/fenToState()/cloneS() never populate it. So s.setupEpMark is truthy IFF we're in setup mode. The guard is redundant; simplified to if(s.setupEpMark)return s.setupEpMark;.
  • Fixed root cause: toggleSetup() exit path did not clear setupEpMark/setupCastleMarks — The guard above only appeared necessary because toggleSetup()'s exit branch (user toggles setup off, rather than tapping Done) did not clear gameState.setupEpMark / gameState.setupCastleMarks. This phase fixes the root cause: added gameState.setupEpMark=null; gameState.setupCastleMarks=new Set(); to the toggle-exit branch, mirroring _exitSetupImpl(). With the root cause fixed, computeVisibleEpMark() needs no setupMode guard at all.
  • Removed misreport comment from _visibleEpMark review-mode guard — const _visibleEpMark=(!reviewMode&&...)?...:null;: the !reviewMode guard is a valid performance optimization (in review mode the main board is covered by .review-overlay, so skipping main-board marker computation saves work), but the old comment '⚡/🔁 markers could theoretically show through the 2% transparent overlay' was the misreport theory. Comment rewritten to describe the performance motivation accurately. Also added the same !reviewMode guard to _visibleCastleMarks (previously only _visibleEpMark had it — inconsistent).
  • Simplified computeVisibleEpMark() enPassantTarget derivation comments — Removed the 'In review mode, after an en passant capture...' misreport context from the defensive pawn verification comments. Kept the valid description: verify the pawn is actually on the expected square with the correct color.
  • Simplified _exitSetupImpl() setupEpMark clear comment — Removed the 'Keeping setupEpMark around would cause computeVisibleEpMark() to return the setup position's pawn square even after moves have been played, causing the ⚡ marker to jump to the wrong position in review mode' misreport theory. Comment now accurately describes: clearing setup-only transient input fields so they don't leak into play/review mode.
  • Simplified enterReview() reviewBaseState derivation comment — Removed the 'v1.0.7 PHASE 9: Always refresh reviewBaseState... leading to ⚡ marker position anomalies in review' misreport theory. Comment now accurately describes: review replays moves from the initial position, so reviewBaseState must be stateHistory[0] (initial position), not gameState (which may be mid-game after an undo). Code logic retained (correct); only comments cleaned up.
  • Simplified enterReview() reviewStates cloneS comments — Three cloneS(s) comments changed from 'v1.0.7 PHASE 9: clone s to prevent shared-reference issues' to accurate descriptions: the null-placeholder and !piece branches REQUIRE cloneS (s is not reassigned, so without clone they'd share the reference); the makeMv success branch's cloneS is defensive (makeMv already returns a fresh object, so the clone is harmless redundancy kept for uniformity across the three push sites).
  • Removed dead variable _boardWidthPx — const _boardWidthPx = _rvCell * 8; was declared but never used; deleted.
🎨 First-Principles Review Conclusions (v1.0.7 Phase 13)
  • enterReview() always derives reviewBaseState from stateHistory[0] — Retained. The code is correct: review replays moves from the initial position, stateHistory[0] is the initial position captured at game start, and gameState is the current position (possibly mid-game after undo). Deriving from stateHistory[0] is the correct design, not a misreport fix.
  • reviewStates entries use cloneS deep copy — Retained. The code is correct: the null-placeholder and !piece branches do not reassign s, so cloneS is required to prevent shared references. The makeMv success branch's cloneS is defensive redundancy (makeMv already returns a fresh object), kept for uniformity across the three push sites.

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 12 Additions (root-cause fix for ⚡ marker displacement on entering Setup mode + root-cause fix for review eval bar width + line-chart minimum-height fix, 2026.6.29)

This phase completes the two remaining v1.0.7 goals: (1) when entering Setup mode, the ⚡ marker now sits on the double-stepped pawn's square rather than on the en-passant capture target square; (2) the review-mode evaluation bar always fills the available width, and the trend chart's minimum height is no less than 80px. Both are first-principles root-cause fixes.

🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 12)
  • ⚡ marker displaced to en-passant capture target square on entering Setup mode (root-cause fix) — Root cause: toggleSetup() seeded the setup marker with gameState.setupEpMark = gameState.enPassantTarget ? {...gameState.enPassantTarget} : null, copying enPassantTarget directly. But the two have different semantics — enPassantTarget is the SKIPPED square (where a capturing pawn lands), while setupEpMark is the square of the double-stepped pawn itself. Direct copy caused the ⚡ marker to render on the wrong square (the en-passant capture target rather than the pawn). Fix: toggleSetup() now reverse-maps enPassantTarget back to the pawn's square — a white pawn double-step produces enPassantTarget.row === 5, with the pawn on row 4; a black pawn double-step produces enPassantTarget.row === 2, with the pawn on row 3. The code also defensively verifies that a pawn of the correct color actually sits on the expected square, so any state inconsistency leaves setupEpMark null instead of producing a misplaced marker.
  • Review-mode evaluation bar did not fill the available width (root-cause fix) — Root cause: in portrait review layout, the eval bar (#review-eval-bar) lives inside .review-left, whose CSS sets align-items:center, causing children to be centered at their natural width rather than stretched to fill. Landscape had an explicit .review-bottom #review-eval-bar { width: 100% } rule, but portrait had no equivalent. Fix: the eval bar's inline style now explicitly sets width:100%; box-sizing:border-box, so it fills its parent's width in both orientations — matching the existing behavior of the trend chart, slider, and nav buttons.
  • Review trend chart minimum height below 80px (root-cause fix) — Root cause: landscape _trendH used Math.max(50, ...) as the lower bound, and CSS .review-chart { min-height: 60px } — both below the 80px readability threshold required by the spec. Fix: landscape _trendH lower bound raised from 50px to 80px; CSS .review-chart min-height raised from 60px to 80px. Portrait was already at 80px minimum; this phase only synchronizes landscape and CSS to match.

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 8 Additions (landscape board oversize fix + dialog button fix + setup marker polish, 2026.6.29)

(Note: the "review mode ⚡ marker position anomaly" fix originally included in this phase was confirmed as a misreport in Phase 13 — the _exitSetupImpl() clear of setupEpMark is retained as correct transient-field cleanup, but its motivation comment has been cleaned up; see the Phase 13 entry.)

🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 8)
  • Landscape board too large, move history panel clipped — Root cause: _recalcCellSize() landscape vertical overhead was only 102px (header + labels + AI bar), not counting player bar (~50px), quick toolbar (~40px), and gaps (~20px) — making the board too tall. Panel minimum width was 180px, too narrow. Fix: vertical overhead raised to 212px; panel minimum width raised to 220px; landscape CELL cap lowered from 90px to 72px, ensuring the move history panel has adequate space.
  • New Game dialog buttons still outside the dialog window — Root cause: portrait CSS set .dlg{height:100%} but behavior under flex align-items:center was uncertain. Fix: added align-self:stretch to ensure .dlg fills .dov's cross axis; .dlg-content uses flex:1 1 auto; .dlg-btns uses flex:0 0 auto to prevent compression.
🎨 Feature Polish (v1.0.7 Phase 8)
  • Setup piece buttons support toggle (click again to deselect) — Clicking the already-selected piece button again deselects it (setupPiece=null), matching the behavior of the 🔁 and ⚡ marker buttons.
  • 🗑️ button is mutually exclusive with 🔁 and ⚡ — Selecting 🗑️ automatically clears any active marker mode; selecting a marker automatically clears 🗑️. The 🗑️ button also supports toggle (click again to deselect).

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 7 Additions (board sizing root-cause fix + dialog layout + setup marker polish, 2026.6.29)

This phase finds the true root cause of the board h-file clipping (.main's padding was never subtracted), fixes the New Game dialog button position and ECO search box display, and polishes several setup-mode marker details.

🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 7)
  • Board h-file cannot be fully displayed (first-principles root-cause fix) — Previously _recalcCellSize() used window.innerWidth to compute available width, but #app has padding-right:calc(env(safe-area-inset-right)+3px) and .main has its own padding:8px (portrait) / 6px (landscape). These paddings were NEVER subtracted, causing the board to be ~16px wider than the actual available space — pushing the h-file past the viewport edge. Fix: _recalcCellSize() now reads #app's clientWidth and subtracts its padding to get the true available content width, then subtracts .main padding, row-label column (28px), board border (4px), and anti-shake margin (6px). Board size now precisely fits the available space.
  • New Game dialog buttons outside the dialog window (root-cause fix) — Previously the portrait CSS set .dlg{height:100vh}, but .dlg is inside .dov which has its own padding. 100vh exceeded .dov's content height, causing the dialog to overflow and buttons to appear outside the window. Fix: changed to height:100% (relative to .dov's content height), so the dialog exactly fills .dov's content area.
  • ECO search box clipped in portrait — Previously the portrait CSS forced the ECO search row (form + select) into a 2-column grid, squeezing the search box. Fix: form and select are now both set to full width (grid-column:1/-1), each on its own row stacked vertically.
  • Setup mode: clicking "Free Play" then exiting causes 🔁 markers to disappear — Root cause: quickFreeOpening() called startGame() which replaced gameState with initState() (no setupCastleMarks) but did NOT clear setupMode. When the user then exited setup, exitSetup() ran on the new gameState, and _validateSetupCastleMarks reset all castling rights to false (no markers). Fix: quickFreeOpening() now clears setupMode and related state BEFORE calling startGame().
🎨 Feature Polish (v1.0.7 Phase 7)
  • ⚡ marker gets "adjacent enemy pawn" legality check — _validateSetupEpMark() now has a 5th rule: the pawn sharing the square with the ⚡ marker must have an adjacent enemy pawn (side-to-move color) on col±1 that can actually capture en passant. If not satisfied, the "⚠️ Cannot complete Setup" notice shows the reason. The setup-mode button tooltip text is updated accordingly. Chinese and English bilingual.

Version number: versionCode=107, versionName="1.0.7" (unchanged). Engine version: Stockfish 18 arm64-v8a-dotprod (unchanged). APK signature: v1+v2+v3 triple-signed, compatible with Xiaomi HyperOS 3. Source tar archive: all engine files excluded.

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 6 Additions (landscape right-edge root-cause fix + setup marker feature polish, 2026.6.29)

This phase finds the true root cause of the landscape right-edge content clipping (CSS box model: width:100% + margin-right causes overflow), and polishes several setup-mode marker feature details.

🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 6)
  • Landscape right-edge content clipping (first-principles root-cause fix) — After 10+ prior failed attempts, found the TRUE root cause: #app used width:100% + margin-right:calc(env(safe-area-inset-right)+3px). In the CSS box model, width:100% makes the element's content-box equal to the parent's content-width; adding a non-zero margin-right then pushes the element's RIGHT EDGE past the parent's right edge by exactly the margin amount. With body's overflow-x:hidden, the rightmost 3px+ of content gets CLIPPED — exactly the "right-edge cut off" symptom users reported in BOTH portrait AND landscape. Fix: moved the safe-area + 3px grip clearance from MARGIN to PADDING on #app. With box-sizing:border-box, width:100% now INCLUDES the padding, so the element's border-box exactly fits the parent (body) content area. No overflow.
  • Setup-mode ⚡-marked pawn could not be captured en passant — Root cause: _validateSetupEpMark() set enPassantTarget to the wrong side of the pawn. White pawns move UP (decreasing row index): from row 6 (rank 2) to row 4 (rank 4), skipping row 5 (rank 3). So for a white pawn on row 4, enPassantTarget should be row 5 (row+1), but the old code set row-1=3 (rank 5, WRONG). Black pawns are the mirror. Fix: white pawn row+1, black pawn row-1, matching makeMv's epRow=(from.row+to.row)/2 calculation.
  • Undo did not correctly restore 🔁/⚡ markers — undoMove() uses cloneS() to restore game state; cloneS() correctly deep-copies castlingRights and enPassantTarget, and markers are derived from these by computeVisibleCastleMarks()/computeVisibleEpMark(). Confirmed the restore chain is correct — this issue was naturally resolved by the enPassantTarget row-number bug fix above (the wrong target square caused the marker to display in the wrong position, which users mistook for "marker not restored").
🎨 UI Optimizations & Feature Polish (v1.0.7 Phase 6)
  • New Game Settings portrait layout completely redesigned — Adopted the standard mobile modal layout: dialog fills the ENTIRE portrait viewport (full width, full height minus safe areas). The Cancel / Start buttons are pinned to the bottom as a sticky footer; the main content area scrolls above and uses the full width — no longer competing with the buttons for horizontal space. Title is pinned to the top. This is the standard mobile-app modal-dialog pattern and optimizes screen-space utilization.
  • ⚡ marker gets a light ultra-thin stroke — Added -webkit-text-stroke:.4px rgba(255,255,255,.7/.85);paint-order:stroke fill to .sq .setup-castle-mark and .sq .setup-ep-mark, improving visibility on both light and dark squares.
  • Setup mode: marker and piece can be placed simultaneously — Marker mode and piece selection are now INDEPENDENT (previously mutually exclusive). The user can select both a piece (e.g. rook) and a marker (e.g. 🔁) simultaneously; clicking a board square places the piece AND toggles the marker in one action. This is convenient for operations like "place a rook and mark it for castling".
  • 🗑️ button gets selected-state highlight — Added .setup-del.act CSS rule with the same gold-border + scale highlight as .setup-btn.act, but keeping the red icon color to indicate it's the delete tool.
  • All setup-mode selectable buttons adapt to Android back button — handleBackPress() now processes in order: marker mode (🔁/⚡) → piece selection (including 🗑️ delete mode) → exit setup. Pressing back first cancels the current selection; pressing again exits setup mode.
🔍 Undo/Redo PGN Cache Consistency (v1.0.7 Phase 6 verification)
  • Undo cache invalidation is complete — undoMove() calls _invalidateCachesForUndoneMoves(moveRecords.length) which clears three caches: (1) _reviewEvalCache (eval cache keyed by reviewStep); (2) _visualAnnotationsCache (visual-annotation cache keyed by moveIdx); (3) _cachedOriginalPGN (imported PGN text, nulled to force _buildPGNString()). _redoStack is preserved to support redo. On redo, cache entries are rebuilt on-demand (evals re-requested, annotations recomputed).

Version number: versionCode=107, versionName="1.0.7" (unchanged). Engine version: Stockfish 18 arm64-v8a-dotprod (unchanged). APK signature: v1+v2+v3 triple-signed, compatible with Xiaomi HyperOS 3. Source tar archive: all engine files excluded.

🆕 v1.0.7 Phase 5 Additions (board sizing and portrait layout optimization, 2026.6.29)

This phase re-examines board sizing and portrait layout from first principles, fixes multiple long-standing display defects, and redesigns the New Game Settings dialog's portrait layout for better space utilization.

🐛 Bug Fixes (v1.0.7 Phase 5)
  • Portrait board h-file clipped — First-principles root-cause analysis: _recalcCellSize() did not subtract three critical clearances when computing available width: (1) the 28px row-label column (.rlbl) sits to the LEFT of the board, pushing the entire board rightward; (2) env(safe-area-inset-right) (non-zero on notched/cutout phones); (3) 3px finger-grip clearance + 4px board border + 6px anti-shake margin. Together these can exceed 41px, causing the board's right edge to be clipped. Fix: added _readSafeInsets() to read actual safe-area insets from CSS custom properties; _recalcCellSize() now fully subtracts all clearances (28px row labels + safe-area left/right + 3px grip + 4px border + 6px anti-shake), guaranteeing the h-file is always fully visible.
  • Landscape right-edge content clipped (regression fix) — The landscape toolbar used overflow-x:auto (horizontal scroll), but was clipped by #app's overflow-x:hidden. Fix: landscape toolbar now uses flex-wrap:wrap (auto-wrap to second row), and .main gets max-width:100%;overflow-x:hidden as a safety net, ensuring all content is fully visible within the viewport.
  • Anti-shake clearance double-counted — .bwrap had margin-right:6px for anti-shake clearance, but _recalcCellSize() also subtracted 6px in the CELL calculation, making the board 6px smaller than necessary. Fix: removed .bwrap's margin-right:6px; anti-shake clearance is now managed solely by _recalcCellSize().
🎨 UI Optimizations (v1.0.7 Phase 5)
  • Board auto-enlarges when space is plentiful — The previous CELL cap was 72px (landscape) / ~50px (portrait), too conservative for large tablets. Fix: cap raised to 90px; tablets and large phones now display a bigger board. Portrait mode now considers BOTH width and height constraints (previously width-only), preventing the board from being too large on ultra-tall phones and pushing below-the-board content out of view.
  • New Game Settings portrait layout redesigned from scratch — Previously ALL flex rows inside .dlg-sec were force-stacked flex-direction:column in portrait, making the dialog very tall and requiring excessive scrolling. Redesign: switched to a 2-column grid layout (grid-template-columns:1fr auto), with labels in the left column and inputs/buttons in the right column — compact and readable. The time-control "base/increment/delay" rows now each occupy one line (label + input side-by-side) instead of label and input each on separate lines. The Chess960 SP-ID row (label + Random button + input+🎲) is also arranged compactly in grid layout. The openings list .op-list max-height is raised to 40vh so users see more openings without scrolling.
  • Landscape toolbar auto-wraps — Previously the landscape toolbar used overflow-x:auto (horizontal scroll), which got clipped under #app overflow-x:hidden. Changed to flex-wrap:wrap (auto-wrap to second row); all buttons are always visible.
